1862       THREAD, NameSigHash*, HASH_ROW_SIZE);
1863     initialize_hashtable(names_and_sigs);
1864     bool dup = false;
1865     const Symbol* name = NULL;
1866     const Symbol* sig = NULL;
1867     {
1868       debug_only(NoSafepointVerifier nsv;)
1869       for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
1870         name = fs.name();
1871         sig = fs.signature();
1872         // If no duplicates, add name/signature in hashtable names_and_sigs.
1873         if (!put_after_lookup(name, sig, names_and_sigs)) {
1874           dup = true;
1875           break;
1876         }
1877       }
1878     }
1879     if (dup) {
1880       classfile_parse_error("Duplicate field name \"%s\" with signature \"%s\" in class file %s",
1881                              name->as_C_string(), sig->as_klass_external_name(), CHECK);
1882     }
1883   }
1884 }
1885 
1886 
1887 const ClassFileParser::unsafe_u2* ClassFileParser::parse_exception_table(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
1888                                                                          u4 code_length,
1889                                                                          u4 exception_table_length,
1890                                                                          TRAPS) {
1891   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
1892 
1893   const unsafe_u2* const exception_table_start = cfs->current();
1894   assert(exception_table_start != NULL, "null exception table");
1895 
1896   cfs->guarantee_more(8 * exception_table_length, CHECK_NULL); // start_pc,
1897                                                                // end_pc,
1898                                                                // handler_pc,
1899                                                                // catch_type_index
1900 
1901   // Will check legal target after parsing code array in verifier.
1902   if (_need_verify) {
1903     for (unsigned int i = 0; i < exception_table_length; i++) {
1904       const u2 start_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1905       const u2 end_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1906       const u2 handler_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1907       const u2 catch_type_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1908       guarantee_property((start_pc < end_pc) && (end_pc <= code_length),
1909                          "Illegal exception table range in class file %s",
1910                          CHECK_NULL);
1911       guarantee_property(handler_pc < code_length,
1912                          "Illegal exception table handler in class file %s",
1913                          CHECK_NULL);
1914       if (catch_type_index != 0) {
1915         guarantee_property(valid_klass_reference_at(catch_type_index),
1916                            "Catch type in exception table has bad constant type in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
1917       }
1918     }
1919   } else {
1920     cfs->skip_u2_fast(exception_table_length * 4);
1921   }
1922   return exception_table_start;
1923 }
1924 
1925 void ClassFileParser::parse_linenumber_table(u4 code_attribute_length,
1926                                              u4 code_length,
1927                                              CompressedLineNumberWriteStream**const write_stream,
1928                                              TRAPS) {
1929 
1930   const ClassFileStream* const cfs = _stream;
1931   unsigned int num_entries = cfs->get_u2(CHECK);
1932 
1933   // Each entry is a u2 start_pc, and a u2 line_number
1934   const unsigned int length_in_bytes = num_entries * (sizeof(u2) * 2);
1935 
1936   // Verify line number attribute and table length
1937   check_property(
1938     code_attribute_length == sizeof(u2) + length_in_bytes,
1939     "LineNumberTable attribute has wrong length in class file %s", CHECK);
1940 
1941   cfs->guarantee_more(length_in_bytes, CHECK);
1942 
1943   if ((*write_stream) == NULL) {
1944     if (length_in_bytes > fixed_buffer_size) {
1945       (*write_stream) = new CompressedLineNumberWriteStream(length_in_bytes);
1946     } else {
1947       (*write_stream) = new CompressedLineNumberWriteStream(
1948         _linenumbertable_buffer, fixed_buffer_size);
1949     }
1950   }
1951 
1952   while (num_entries-- > 0) {
1953     const u2 bci  = cfs->get_u2_fast(); // start_pc
1954     const u2 line = cfs->get_u2_fast(); // line_number
1955     guarantee_property(bci < code_length,
1956         "Invalid pc in LineNumberTable in class file %s", CHECK);
1957     (*write_stream)->write_pair(bci, line);
1958   }
1959 }
1960 
1961 
1962 class LVT_Hash : public AllStatic {
1963  public:
1964 
1965   static bool equals(LocalVariableTableElement const& e0, LocalVariableTableElement const& e1) {
1966   /*
1967    * 3-tuple start_bci/length/slot has to be unique key,
1968    * so the following comparison seems to be redundant:
1969    *       && elem->name_cp_index == entry->_elem->name_cp_index
1970    */
1971     return (e0.start_bci     == e1.start_bci &&
1972             e0.length        == e1.length &&
1973             e0.name_cp_index == e1.name_cp_index &&
1974             e0.slot          == e1.slot);
1975   }
1976 
1977   static unsigned int hash(LocalVariableTableElement const& e0) {
1978     unsigned int raw_hash = e0.start_bci;
1979 
1980     raw_hash = e0.length        + raw_hash * 37;
1981     raw_hash = e0.name_cp_index + raw_hash * 37;
1982     raw_hash = e0.slot          + raw_hash * 37;
1983 
1984     return raw_hash;
1985   }
1986 };
1987 
1988 
1989 // Class file LocalVariableTable elements.
1990 class Classfile_LVT_Element {
1991  public:
1992   u2 start_bci;
1993   u2 length;
1994   u2 name_cp_index;
1995   u2 descriptor_cp_index;
1996   u2 slot;
1997 };
1998 
1999 static void copy_lvt_element(const Classfile_LVT_Element* const src,
2000                              LocalVariableTableElement* const lvt) {
2001   lvt->start_bci           = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->start_bci);
2002   lvt->length              = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->length);
2003   lvt->name_cp_index       = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->name_cp_index);
2004   lvt->descriptor_cp_index = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->descriptor_cp_index);
2005   lvt->signature_cp_index  = 0;
2006   lvt->slot                = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->slot);
2007 }
2008 
2009 // Function is used to parse both attributes:
2010 // LocalVariableTable (LVT) and LocalVariableTypeTable (LVTT)
2011 const ClassFileParser::unsafe_u2* ClassFileParser::parse_localvariable_table(const ClassFileStream* cfs,
2012                                                                              u4 code_length,
2013                                                                              u2 max_locals,
2014                                                                              u4 code_attribute_length,
2015                                                                              u2* const localvariable_table_length,
2016                                                                              bool isLVTT,
2017                                                                              TRAPS) {
2018   const char* const tbl_name = (isLVTT) ? "LocalVariableTypeTable" : "LocalVariableTable";
2019   *localvariable_table_length = cfs->get_u2(CHECK_NULL);
2020   const unsigned int size =
2021     (*localvariable_table_length) * sizeof(Classfile_LVT_Element) / sizeof(u2);
2022 
2023   const ConstantPool* const cp = _cp;
2024 
2025   // Verify local variable table attribute has right length
2026   if (_need_verify) {
2027     guarantee_property(code_attribute_length == (sizeof(*localvariable_table_length) + size * sizeof(u2)),
2028                        "%s has wrong length in class file %s", tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2029   }
2030 
2031   const unsafe_u2* const localvariable_table_start = cfs->current();
2032   assert(localvariable_table_start != NULL, "null local variable table");
2033   if (!_need_verify) {
2034     cfs->skip_u2_fast(size);
2035   } else {
2036     cfs->guarantee_more(size * 2, CHECK_NULL);
2037     for(int i = 0; i < (*localvariable_table_length); i++) {
2038       const u2 start_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2039       const u2 length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2040       const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2041       const u2 descriptor_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2042       const u2 index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2043       // Assign to a u4 to avoid overflow
2044       const u4 end_pc = (u4)start_pc + (u4)length;
2045 
2046       if (start_pc >= code_length) {
2047         classfile_parse_error(
2048           "Invalid start_pc %u in %s in class file %s",
2049           start_pc, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2050       }
2051       if (end_pc > code_length) {
2052         classfile_parse_error(
2053           "Invalid length %u in %s in class file %s",
2054           length, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2055       }
2056       const int cp_size = cp->length();
2057       guarantee_property(valid_symbol_at(name_index),
2058         "Name index %u in %s has bad constant type in class file %s",
2059         name_index, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2060       guarantee_property(valid_symbol_at(descriptor_index),
2061         "Signature index %u in %s has bad constant type in class file %s",
2062         descriptor_index, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2063 
2064       const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_index);
2065       const Symbol* const sig = cp->symbol_at(descriptor_index);
2066       verify_legal_field_name(name, CHECK_NULL);
2067       u2 extra_slot = 0;
2068       if (!isLVTT) {
2069         verify_legal_field_signature(name, sig, CHECK_NULL);
2070 
2071         // 4894874: check special cases for double and long local variables
2072         if (sig == vmSymbols::type_signature(T_DOUBLE) ||
2073             sig == vmSymbols::type_signature(T_LONG)) {
2074           extra_slot = 1;
2075         }
2076       }
2077       guarantee_property((index + extra_slot) < max_locals,
2078                           "Invalid index %u in %s in class file %s",
2079                           index, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2080     }
2081   }
2082   return localvariable_table_start;
2083 }
2084 
2085 static const u1* parse_stackmap_table(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
2086                                       u4 code_attribute_length,
2087                                       bool need_verify,
2088                                       TRAPS) {
2089   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
2090 
2091   if (0 == code_attribute_length) {
2092     return NULL;
2093   }
2094 
2095   const u1* const stackmap_table_start = cfs->current();
2096   assert(stackmap_table_start != NULL, "null stackmap table");
2097 
2098   // check code_attribute_length first
2099   cfs->skip_u1(code_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2100 
2101   if (!need_verify && !DumpSharedSpaces) {
2102     return NULL;
2103   }
2104   return stackmap_table_start;
2105 }
2106 
2107 const ClassFileParser::unsafe_u2* ClassFileParser::parse_checked_exceptions(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
2108                                                                             u2* const checked_exceptions_length,
2109                                                                             u4 method_attribute_length,
2110                                                                             TRAPS) {
2111   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
2112   assert(checked_exceptions_length != NULL, "invariant");
2113 
2114   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_NULL);  // checked_exceptions_length
2115   *checked_exceptions_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2116   const unsigned int size =
2117     (*checked_exceptions_length) * sizeof(CheckedExceptionElement) / sizeof(u2);
2118   const unsafe_u2* const checked_exceptions_start = cfs->current();
2119   assert(checked_exceptions_start != NULL, "null checked exceptions");
2120   if (!_need_verify) {
2121     cfs->skip_u2_fast(size);
2122   } else {
2123     // Verify each value in the checked exception table
2124     u2 checked_exception;
2125     const u2 len = *checked_exceptions_length;
2126     cfs->guarantee_more(2 * len, CHECK_NULL);
2127     for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
2128       checked_exception = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2129       check_property(
2130         valid_klass_reference_at(checked_exception),
2131         "Exception name has bad type at constant pool %u in class file %s",
2132         checked_exception, CHECK_NULL);
2133     }
2134   }
2135   // check exceptions attribute length
2136   if (_need_verify) {
2137     guarantee_property(method_attribute_length == (sizeof(*checked_exceptions_length) +
2138                                                    sizeof(u2) * size),
2139                       "Exceptions attribute has wrong length in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2140   }
2141   return checked_exceptions_start;
2142 }
2143 
2144 void ClassFileParser::throwIllegalSignature(const char* type,
2145                                             const Symbol* name,
2146                                             const Symbol* sig,
2147                                             TRAPS) const {
2148   assert(name != NULL, "invariant");
2149   assert(sig != NULL, "invariant");
2150 
2151   const char* class_note = "";
2152   if (is_inline_type() && name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
2153     class_note = " (an inline class)";
2154   }
2155 
2156   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
2157   Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
2158       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
2159       "%s \"%s\" in class %s%s has illegal signature \"%s\"", type,
2160       name->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, sig->as_C_string());
2161 }
2162 
2163 AnnotationCollector::ID
2164 AnnotationCollector::annotation_index(const ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
2165                                       const Symbol* name,
2166                                       const bool can_access_vm_annotations) {
2167   const vmSymbols::SID sid = vmSymbols::find_sid(name);
2168   // Privileged code can use all annotations.  Other code silently drops some.
2169   const bool privileged = loader_data->is_boot_class_loader_data() ||
2170                           loader_data->is_platform_class_loader_data() ||
2171                           can_access_vm_annotations;
2172   switch (sid) {
2173     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(reflect_CallerSensitive_signature): {
2174       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2175       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2176       return _method_CallerSensitive;
2177     }
2178     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ForceInline_signature): {
2179       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2180       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2181       return _method_ForceInline;
2182     }
2183     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_DontInline_signature): {
2184       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2185       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2186       return _method_DontInline;
2187     }
2188     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(java_lang_invoke_InjectedProfile_signature): {
2189       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2190       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2191       return _method_InjectedProfile;
2192     }
2193     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(java_lang_invoke_LambdaForm_Compiled_signature): {
2194       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2195       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2196       return _method_LambdaForm_Compiled;
2197     }
2198     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Hidden_signature): {
2199       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2200       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2201       return _method_Hidden;
2202     }
2203     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate_signature): {
2204       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2205       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2206       return _method_HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate;
2207     }
2208     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Stable_signature): {
2209       if (_location != _in_field)   break;  // only allow for fields
2210       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2211       return _field_Stable;
2212     }
2213     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Contended_signature): {
2214       if (_location != _in_field && _location != _in_class) {
2215         break;  // only allow for fields and classes
2216       }
2217       if (!EnableContended || (RestrictContended && !privileged)) {
2218         break;  // honor privileges
2219       }
2220       return _jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Contended;
2221     }
2222     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ReservedStackAccess_signature): {
2223       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2224       if (RestrictReservedStack && !privileged) break; // honor privileges
2225       return _jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ReservedStackAccess;
2226     }
2227     default: {
2228       break;
2229     }
2230   }
2231   return AnnotationCollector::_unknown;
2232 }
2233 
2234 void ClassFileParser::FieldAnnotationCollector::apply_to(FieldInfo* f) {
2235   if (is_contended())
2236     f->set_contended_group(contended_group());
2237   if (is_stable())
2238     f->set_stable(true);
2239 }
2240 
2241 ClassFileParser::FieldAnnotationCollector::~FieldAnnotationCollector() {
2242   // If there's an error deallocate metadata for field annotations
2243   MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _field_annotations);
2244   MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _field_type_annotations);
2245 }
2246 
2247 void MethodAnnotationCollector::apply_to(const methodHandle& m) {
2248   if (has_annotation(_method_CallerSensitive))
2249     m->set_caller_sensitive(true);
2250   if (has_annotation(_method_ForceInline))
2251     m->set_force_inline(true);
2252   if (has_annotation(_method_DontInline))
2253     m->set_dont_inline(true);
2254   if (has_annotation(_method_InjectedProfile))
2255     m->set_has_injected_profile(true);
2256   if (has_annotation(_method_LambdaForm_Compiled) && m->intrinsic_id() == vmIntrinsics::_none)
2257     m->set_intrinsic_id(vmIntrinsics::_compiledLambdaForm);
2258   if (has_annotation(_method_Hidden))
2259     m->set_hidden(true);
2260   if (has_annotation(_method_HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate) && !m->is_synthetic())
2261     m->set_intrinsic_candidate(true);
2262   if (has_annotation(_jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ReservedStackAccess))
2263     m->set_has_reserved_stack_access(true);
2264 }
2265 
2266 void ClassFileParser::ClassAnnotationCollector::apply_to(InstanceKlass* ik) {
2267   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
2268   ik->set_is_contended(is_contended());
2269 }
2270 
2271 #define MAX_ARGS_SIZE 255
2272 #define MAX_CODE_SIZE 65535
2273 #define INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER 256
2274 
2275 /* Copy class file LVT's/LVTT's into the HotSpot internal LVT.
2276  *
2277  * Rules for LVT's and LVTT's are:
2278  *   - There can be any number of LVT's and LVTT's.
2279  *   - If there are n LVT's, it is the same as if there was just
2280  *     one LVT containing all the entries from the n LVT's.
2281  *   - There may be no more than one LVT entry per local variable.
2282  *     Two LVT entries are 'equal' if these fields are the same:
2283  *        start_pc, length, name, slot
2284  *   - There may be no more than one LVTT entry per each LVT entry.
2285  *     Each LVTT entry has to match some LVT entry.
2286  *   - HotSpot internal LVT keeps natural ordering of class file LVT entries.
2287  */
2288 void ClassFileParser::copy_localvariable_table(const ConstMethod* cm,
2289                                                int lvt_cnt,
2290                                                u2* const localvariable_table_length,
2291                                                const unsafe_u2** const localvariable_table_start,
2292                                                int lvtt_cnt,
2293                                                u2* const localvariable_type_table_length,
2294                                                const unsafe_u2** const localvariable_type_table_start,
2295                                                TRAPS) {
2296 
2297   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
2298 
2299   typedef ResourceHashtable<LocalVariableTableElement, LocalVariableTableElement*,
2300                             &LVT_Hash::hash, &LVT_Hash::equals> LVT_HashTable;
2301 
2302   LVT_HashTable* const table = new LVT_HashTable();
2303 
2304   // To fill LocalVariableTable in
2305   const Classfile_LVT_Element* cf_lvt;
2306   LocalVariableTableElement* lvt = cm->localvariable_table_start();
2307 
2308   for (int tbl_no = 0; tbl_no < lvt_cnt; tbl_no++) {
2309     cf_lvt = (Classfile_LVT_Element *) localvariable_table_start[tbl_no];
2310     for (int idx = 0; idx < localvariable_table_length[tbl_no]; idx++, lvt++) {
2311       copy_lvt_element(&cf_lvt[idx], lvt);
2312       // If no duplicates, add LVT elem in hashtable.
2313       if (table->put(*lvt, lvt) == false
2314           && _need_verify
2315           && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
2316         classfile_parse_error("Duplicated LocalVariableTable attribute "
2317                               "entry for '%s' in class file %s",
2318                                _cp->symbol_at(lvt->name_cp_index)->as_utf8(),
2319                                CHECK);
2320       }
2321     }
2322   }
2323 
2324   // To merge LocalVariableTable and LocalVariableTypeTable
2325   const Classfile_LVT_Element* cf_lvtt;
2326   LocalVariableTableElement lvtt_elem;
2327 
2328   for (int tbl_no = 0; tbl_no < lvtt_cnt; tbl_no++) {
2329     cf_lvtt = (Classfile_LVT_Element *) localvariable_type_table_start[tbl_no];
2330     for (int idx = 0; idx < localvariable_type_table_length[tbl_no]; idx++) {
2331       copy_lvt_element(&cf_lvtt[idx], &lvtt_elem);
2332       LocalVariableTableElement** entry = table->get(lvtt_elem);
2333       if (entry == NULL) {
2334         if (_need_verify) {
2335           classfile_parse_error("LVTT entry for '%s' in class file %s "
2336                                 "does not match any LVT entry",
2337                                  _cp->symbol_at(lvtt_elem.name_cp_index)->as_utf8(),
2338                                  CHECK);
2339         }
2340       } else if ((*entry)->signature_cp_index != 0 && _need_verify) {
2341         classfile_parse_error("Duplicated LocalVariableTypeTable attribute "
2342                               "entry for '%s' in class file %s",
2343                                _cp->symbol_at(lvtt_elem.name_cp_index)->as_utf8(),
2344                                CHECK);
2345       } else {
2346         // to add generic signatures into LocalVariableTable
2347         (*entry)->signature_cp_index = lvtt_elem.descriptor_cp_index;
2348       }
2349     }
2350   }
2351 }
2352 
2353 
2354 void ClassFileParser::copy_method_annotations(ConstMethod* cm,
2355                                        const u1* runtime_visible_annotations,
2356                                        int runtime_visible_annotations_length,
2357                                        const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations,
2358                                        int runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
2359                                        const u1* runtime_visible_parameter_annotations,
2360                                        int runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length,
2361                                        const u1* runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations,
2362                                        int runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
2363                                        const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations,
2364                                        int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
2365                                        const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
2366                                        int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
2367                                        const u1* annotation_default,
2368                                        int annotation_default_length,
2369                                        TRAPS) {
2370 
2371   AnnotationArray* a;
2372 
2373   if (runtime_visible_annotations_length +
2374       runtime_invisible_annotations_length > 0) {
2375      a = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
2376                               runtime_visible_annotations_length,
2377                               runtime_invisible_annotations,
2378                               runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
2379                               CHECK);
2380      cm->set_method_annotations(a);
2381   }
2382 
2383   if (runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length +
2384       runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length > 0) {
2385     a = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_parameter_annotations,
2386                              runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length,
2387                              runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations,
2388                              runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
2389                              CHECK);
2390     cm->set_parameter_annotations(a);
2391   }
2392 
2393   if (annotation_default_length > 0) {
2394     a = assemble_annotations(annotation_default,
2395                              annotation_default_length,
2396                              NULL,
2397                              0,
2398                              CHECK);
2399     cm->set_default_annotations(a);
2400   }
2401 
2402   if (runtime_visible_type_annotations_length +
2403       runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length > 0) {
2404     a = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
2405                              runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
2406                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
2407                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
2408                              CHECK);
2409     cm->set_type_annotations(a);
2410   }
2411 }
2412 
2413 
2414 // Note: the parse_method below is big and clunky because all parsing of the code and exceptions
2415 // attribute is inlined. This is cumbersome to avoid since we inline most of the parts in the
2416 // Method* to save footprint, so we only know the size of the resulting Method* when the
2417 // entire method attribute is parsed.
2418 //
2419 // The promoted_flags parameter is used to pass relevant access_flags
2420 // from the method back up to the containing klass. These flag values
2421 // are added to klass's access_flags.
2422 
2423 Method* ClassFileParser::parse_method(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
2424                                       bool is_interface,
2425                                       bool is_inline_type,
2426                                       const ConstantPool* cp,
2427                                       AccessFlags* const promoted_flags,
2428                                       TRAPS) {
2429   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
2430   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
2431   assert(promoted_flags != NULL, "invariant");
2432 
2433   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
2434   // Parse fixed parts:
2435   // access_flags, name_index, descriptor_index, attributes_count
2436   cfs->guarantee_more(8, CHECK_NULL);
2437 
2438   int flags = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2439   const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2440   const int cp_size = cp->length();
2441   check_property(
2442     valid_symbol_at(name_index),
2443     "Illegal constant pool index %u for method name in class file %s",
2444     name_index, CHECK_NULL);
2445   const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_index);
2446   verify_legal_method_name(name, CHECK_NULL);
2447 
2448   const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2449   guarantee_property(
2450     valid_symbol_at(signature_index),
2451     "Illegal constant pool index %u for method signature in class file %s",
2452     signature_index, CHECK_NULL);
2453   const Symbol* const signature = cp->symbol_at(signature_index);
2454 
2455   if (name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name()) {
2456     // We ignore the other access flags for a valid class initializer.
2457     // (JVM Spec 2nd ed., chapter 4.6)
2458     if (_major_version < 51) { // backward compatibility
2459       flags = JVM_ACC_STATIC;
2460     } else if ((flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC) == JVM_ACC_STATIC) {
2461       flags &= JVM_ACC_STATIC | JVM_ACC_STRICT;
2462     } else {
2463       classfile_parse_error("Method <clinit> is not static in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2464     }
2465   } else {
2466     verify_legal_method_modifiers(flags, is_interface, is_inline_type, name, CHECK_NULL);
2467   }
2468 
2469   if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
2470     if (is_interface) {
2471       classfile_parse_error("Interface cannot have a method named <init>, class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2472     } else if (!is_inline_type && signature->is_void_method_signature()) {
2473       // OK, a constructor
2474     } else if (is_inline_type && !signature->is_void_method_signature()) {
2475       // also OK, a static factory, as long as the return value is good
2476       bool ok = false;
2477       SignatureStream ss((Symbol*) signature, true);
2478       while (!ss.at_return_type())  ss.next();
2479       if (ss.is_reference()) {
2480         Symbol* ret = ss.as_symbol();
2481         const Symbol* required = class_name();
2482         if (is_hidden() || is_unsafe_anonymous()) {
2483           // The original class name in hidden classes and in the UAC byte stream gets
2484           // changed.  So using the original name in the return type is no longer valid.
2485           required = vmSymbols::java_lang_Object();
2486         }
2487         ok = (ret == required);
2488       }
2489       if (!ok) {
2490         throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
2491       }
2492     } else {
2493       // not OK, so throw the same error as in verify_legal_method_signature.
2494       throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
2495     }
2496     // A declared <init> method must always be either a non-static
2497     // object constructor, with a void return, or else it must be a
2498     // static factory method, with a non-void return.  No other
2499     // definition of <init> is possible.
2500     //
2501     // The verifier (in verify_invoke_instructions) will inspect the
2502     // signature of any attempt to invoke <init>, and ensures that it
2503     // returns non-void if and only if it is being invoked by
2504     // invokestatic, and void if and only if it is being invoked by
2505     // invokespecial.
2506     //
2507     // When a symbolic reference to <init> is resolved for a
2508     // particular invocation mode (special or static), the mode is
2509     // matched to the JVM_ACC_STATIC modifier of the <init> method.
2510     // Thus, it is impossible to statically invoke a constructor, and
2511     // impossible to "new + invokespecial" a static factory, either
2512     // through bytecode or through reflection.
2513   }
2514 
2515   int args_size = -1;  // only used when _need_verify is true
2516   if (_need_verify) {
2517     args_size = ((flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC) ? 0 : 1) +
2518                  verify_legal_method_signature(name, signature, CHECK_NULL);
2519     if (args_size > MAX_ARGS_SIZE) {
2520       classfile_parse_error("Too many arguments in method signature in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2521     }
2522   }
2523 
2524   AccessFlags access_flags(flags & JVM_RECOGNIZED_METHOD_MODIFIERS);
2525 
2526   // Default values for code and exceptions attribute elements
2527   u2 max_stack = 0;
2528   u2 max_locals = 0;
2529   u4 code_length = 0;
2530   const u1* code_start = 0;
2531   u2 exception_table_length = 0;
2532   const unsafe_u2* exception_table_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to array of u2 elements
2533   Array<int>* exception_handlers = Universe::the_empty_int_array();
2534   u2 checked_exceptions_length = 0;
2535   const unsafe_u2* checked_exceptions_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to array of u2 elements
2536   CompressedLineNumberWriteStream* linenumber_table = NULL;
2537   int linenumber_table_length = 0;
2538   int total_lvt_length = 0;
2539   u2 lvt_cnt = 0;
2540   u2 lvtt_cnt = 0;
2541   bool lvt_allocated = false;
2542   u2 max_lvt_cnt = INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER;
2543   u2 max_lvtt_cnt = INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER;
2544   u2* localvariable_table_length = NULL;
2545   const unsafe_u2** localvariable_table_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to array of LVT attributes
2546   u2* localvariable_type_table_length = NULL;
2547   const unsafe_u2** localvariable_type_table_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to LVTT attributes
2548   int method_parameters_length = -1;
2549   const u1* method_parameters_data = NULL;
2550   bool method_parameters_seen = false;
2551   bool parsed_code_attribute = false;
2552   bool parsed_checked_exceptions_attribute = false;
2553   bool parsed_stackmap_attribute = false;
2554   // stackmap attribute - JDK1.5
2555   const u1* stackmap_data = NULL;
2556   int stackmap_data_length = 0;
2557   u2 generic_signature_index = 0;
2558   MethodAnnotationCollector parsed_annotations;
2559   const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
2560   int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
2561   const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
2562   int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
2563   const u1* runtime_visible_parameter_annotations = NULL;
2564   int runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length = 0;
2565   const u1* runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations = NULL;
2566   int runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length = 0;
2567   const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
2568   int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
2569   const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
2570   int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
2571   bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
2572   bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
2573   bool runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_exists = false;
2574   const u1* annotation_default = NULL;
2575   int annotation_default_length = 0;
2576 
2577   // Parse code and exceptions attribute
2578   u2 method_attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2579   while (method_attributes_count--) {
2580     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_NULL);  // method_attribute_name_index, method_attribute_length
2581     const u2 method_attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2582     const u4 method_attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
2583     check_property(
2584       valid_symbol_at(method_attribute_name_index),
2585       "Invalid method attribute name index %u in class file %s",
2586       method_attribute_name_index, CHECK_NULL);
2587 
2588     const Symbol* const method_attribute_name = cp->symbol_at(method_attribute_name_index);
2589     if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_code()) {
2590       // Parse Code attribute
2591       if (_need_verify) {
2592         guarantee_property(
2593             !access_flags.is_native() && !access_flags.is_abstract(),
2594                         "Code attribute in native or abstract methods in class file %s",
2595                          CHECK_NULL);
2596       }
2597       if (parsed_code_attribute) {
2598         classfile_parse_error("Multiple Code attributes in class file %s",
2599                               CHECK_NULL);
2600       }
2601       parsed_code_attribute = true;
2602 
2603       // Stack size, locals size, and code size
2604       cfs->guarantee_more(8, CHECK_NULL);
2605       max_stack = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2606       max_locals = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2607       code_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
2608       if (_need_verify) {
2609         guarantee_property(args_size <= max_locals,
2610                            "Arguments can't fit into locals in class file %s",
2611                            CHECK_NULL);
2612         guarantee_property(code_length > 0 && code_length <= MAX_CODE_SIZE,
2613                            "Invalid method Code length %u in class file %s",
2614                            code_length, CHECK_NULL);
2615       }
2616       // Code pointer
2617       code_start = cfs->current();
2618       assert(code_start != NULL, "null code start");
2619       cfs->guarantee_more(code_length, CHECK_NULL);
2620       cfs->skip_u1_fast(code_length);
2621 
2622       // Exception handler table
2623       cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_NULL);  // exception_table_length
2624       exception_table_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2625       if (exception_table_length > 0) {
2626         exception_table_start = parse_exception_table(cfs,
2627                                                       code_length,
2628                                                       exception_table_length,
2629                                                       CHECK_NULL);
2630       }
2631 
2632       // Parse additional attributes in code attribute
2633       cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_NULL);  // code_attributes_count
2634       u2 code_attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2635 
2636       unsigned int calculated_attribute_length = 0;
2637 
2638       calculated_attribute_length =
2639           sizeof(max_stack) + sizeof(max_locals) + sizeof(code_length);
2640       calculated_attribute_length +=
2641         code_length +
2642         sizeof(exception_table_length) +
2643         sizeof(code_attributes_count) +
2644         exception_table_length *
2645             ( sizeof(u2) +   // start_pc
2646               sizeof(u2) +   // end_pc
2647               sizeof(u2) +   // handler_pc
2648               sizeof(u2) );  // catch_type_index
2649 
2650       while (code_attributes_count--) {
2651         cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_NULL);  // code_attribute_name_index, code_attribute_length
2652         const u2 code_attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2653         const u4 code_attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
2654         calculated_attribute_length += code_attribute_length +
2655                                        sizeof(code_attribute_name_index) +
2656                                        sizeof(code_attribute_length);
2657         check_property(valid_symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index),
2658                        "Invalid code attribute name index %u in class file %s",
2659                        code_attribute_name_index,
2660                        CHECK_NULL);
2661         if (LoadLineNumberTables &&
2662             cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_line_number_table()) {
2663           // Parse and compress line number table
2664           parse_linenumber_table(code_attribute_length,
2665                                  code_length,
2666                                  &linenumber_table,
2667                                  CHECK_NULL);
2668 
2669         } else if (LoadLocalVariableTables &&
2670                    cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_local_variable_table()) {
2671           // Parse local variable table
2672           if (!lvt_allocated) {
2673             localvariable_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2674               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2675             localvariable_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2676               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2677             localvariable_type_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2678               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2679             localvariable_type_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2680               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2681             lvt_allocated = true;
2682           }
2683           if (lvt_cnt == max_lvt_cnt) {
2684             max_lvt_cnt <<= 1;
2685             localvariable_table_length = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(u2, localvariable_table_length, lvt_cnt, max_lvt_cnt);
2686             localvariable_table_start  = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(const unsafe_u2*, localvariable_table_start, lvt_cnt, max_lvt_cnt);
2687           }
2688           localvariable_table_start[lvt_cnt] =
2689             parse_localvariable_table(cfs,
2690                                       code_length,
2691                                       max_locals,
2692                                       code_attribute_length,
2693                                       &localvariable_table_length[lvt_cnt],
2694                                       false,    // is not LVTT
2695                                       CHECK_NULL);
2696           total_lvt_length += localvariable_table_length[lvt_cnt];
2697           lvt_cnt++;
2698         } else if (LoadLocalVariableTypeTables &&
2699                    _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION &&
2700                    cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_local_variable_type_table()) {
2701           if (!lvt_allocated) {
2702             localvariable_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2703               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2704             localvariable_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2705               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2706             localvariable_type_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2707               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2708             localvariable_type_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2709               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2710             lvt_allocated = true;
2711           }
2712           // Parse local variable type table
2713           if (lvtt_cnt == max_lvtt_cnt) {
2714             max_lvtt_cnt <<= 1;
2715             localvariable_type_table_length = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(u2, localvariable_type_table_length, lvtt_cnt, max_lvtt_cnt);
2716             localvariable_type_table_start  = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(const unsafe_u2*, localvariable_type_table_start, lvtt_cnt, max_lvtt_cnt);
2717           }
2718           localvariable_type_table_start[lvtt_cnt] =
2719             parse_localvariable_table(cfs,
2720                                       code_length,
2721                                       max_locals,
2722                                       code_attribute_length,
2723                                       &localvariable_type_table_length[lvtt_cnt],
2724                                       true,     // is LVTT
2725                                       CHECK_NULL);
2726           lvtt_cnt++;
2727         } else if (_major_version >= Verifier::STACKMAP_ATTRIBUTE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
2728                    cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_stack_map_table()) {
2729           // Stack map is only needed by the new verifier in JDK1.5.
2730           if (parsed_stackmap_attribute) {
2731             classfile_parse_error("Multiple StackMapTable attributes in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2732           }
2733           stackmap_data = parse_stackmap_table(cfs, code_attribute_length, _need_verify, CHECK_NULL);
2734           stackmap_data_length = code_attribute_length;
2735           parsed_stackmap_attribute = true;
2736         } else {
2737           // Skip unknown attributes
2738           cfs->skip_u1(code_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2739         }
2740       }
2741       // check method attribute length
2742       if (_need_verify) {
2743         guarantee_property(method_attribute_length == calculated_attribute_length,
2744                            "Code segment has wrong length in class file %s",
2745                            CHECK_NULL);
2746       }
2747     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_exceptions()) {
2748       // Parse Exceptions attribute
2749       if (parsed_checked_exceptions_attribute) {
2750         classfile_parse_error("Multiple Exceptions attributes in class file %s",
2751                               CHECK_NULL);
2752       }
2753       parsed_checked_exceptions_attribute = true;
2754       checked_exceptions_start =
2755             parse_checked_exceptions(cfs,
2756                                      &checked_exceptions_length,
2757                                      method_attribute_length,
2758                                      CHECK_NULL);
2759     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_method_parameters()) {
2760       // reject multiple method parameters
2761       if (method_parameters_seen) {
2762         classfile_parse_error("Multiple MethodParameters attributes in class file %s",
2763                               CHECK_NULL);
2764       }
2765       method_parameters_seen = true;
2766       method_parameters_length = cfs->get_u1_fast();
2767       const u2 real_length = (method_parameters_length * 4u) + 1u;
2768       if (method_attribute_length != real_length) {
2769         classfile_parse_error(
2770           "Invalid MethodParameters method attribute length %u in class file",
2771           method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2772       }
2773       method_parameters_data = cfs->current();
2774       cfs->skip_u2_fast(method_parameters_length);
2775       cfs->skip_u2_fast(method_parameters_length);
2776       // ignore this attribute if it cannot be reflected
2777       if (!SystemDictionary::Parameter_klass_loaded())
2778         method_parameters_length = -1;
2779     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_synthetic()) {
2780       if (method_attribute_length != 0) {
2781         classfile_parse_error(
2782           "Invalid Synthetic method attribute length %u in class file %s",
2783           method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2784       }
2785       // Should we check that there hasn't already been a synthetic attribute?
2786       access_flags.set_is_synthetic();
2787     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_deprecated()) { // 4276120
2788       if (method_attribute_length != 0) {
2789         classfile_parse_error(
2790           "Invalid Deprecated method attribute length %u in class file %s",
2791           method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2792       }
2793     } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
2794       if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
2795         if (generic_signature_index != 0) {
2796           classfile_parse_error(
2797             "Multiple Signature attributes for method in class file %s",
2798             CHECK_NULL);
2799         }
2800         if (method_attribute_length != 2) {
2801           classfile_parse_error(
2802             "Invalid Signature attribute length %u in class file %s",
2803             method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2804         }
2805         generic_signature_index = parse_generic_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK_NULL);
2806       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
2807         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
2808           classfile_parse_error(
2809             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2810             CHECK_NULL);
2811         }
2812         runtime_visible_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2813         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
2814         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null visible annotations");
2815         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK_NULL);
2816         parse_annotations(cp,
2817                           runtime_visible_annotations,
2818                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
2819                           &parsed_annotations,
2820                           _loader_data,
2821                           _can_access_vm_annotations,
2822                           CHECK_NULL);
2823         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
2824       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
2825         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
2826           classfile_parse_error(
2827             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2828             CHECK_NULL);
2829         }
2830         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
2831         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
2832           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2833           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
2834           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null invisible annotations");
2835         }
2836         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2837       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_parameter_annotations()) {
2838         if (runtime_visible_parameter_annotations != NULL) {
2839           classfile_parse_error(
2840             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleParameterAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2841             CHECK_NULL);
2842         }
2843         runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2844         runtime_visible_parameter_annotations = cfs->current();
2845         assert(runtime_visible_parameter_annotations != NULL, "null visible parameter annotations");
2846         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length, CHECK_NULL);
2847       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations()) {
2848         if (runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_exists) {
2849           classfile_parse_error(
2850             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleParameterAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2851             CHECK_NULL);
2852         }
2853         runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_exists = true;
2854         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
2855           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2856           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations = cfs->current();
2857           assert(runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations != NULL,
2858             "null invisible parameter annotations");
2859         }
2860         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2861       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_annotation_default()) {
2862         if (annotation_default != NULL) {
2863           classfile_parse_error(
2864             "Multiple AnnotationDefault attributes for method in class file %s",
2865             CHECK_NULL);
2866         }
2867         annotation_default_length = method_attribute_length;
2868         annotation_default = cfs->current();
2869         assert(annotation_default != NULL, "null annotation default");
2870         cfs->skip_u1(annotation_default_length, CHECK_NULL);
2871       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
2872         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
2873           classfile_parse_error(
2874             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2875             CHECK_NULL);
2876         }
2877         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2878         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
2879         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null visible type annotations");
2880         // No need for the VM to parse Type annotations
2881         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK_NULL);
2882       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
2883         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
2884           classfile_parse_error(
2885             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2886             CHECK_NULL);
2887         } else {
2888           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
2889         }
2890         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
2891           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2892           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
2893           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null invisible type annotations");
2894         }
2895         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2896       } else {
2897         // Skip unknown attributes
2898         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2899       }
2900     } else {
2901       // Skip unknown attributes
2902       cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2903     }
2904   }
2905 
2906   if (linenumber_table != NULL) {
2907     linenumber_table->write_terminator();
2908     linenumber_table_length = linenumber_table->position();
2909   }
2910 
2911   // Make sure there's at least one Code attribute in non-native/non-abstract method
2912   if (_need_verify) {
2913     guarantee_property(access_flags.is_native() ||
2914                        access_flags.is_abstract() ||
2915                        parsed_code_attribute,
2916                        "Absent Code attribute in method that is not native or abstract in class file %s",
2917                        CHECK_NULL);
2918   }
2919 
2920   // All sizing information for a Method* is finally available, now create it
2921   InlineTableSizes sizes(
2922       total_lvt_length,
2923       linenumber_table_length,
2924       exception_table_length,
2925       checked_exceptions_length,
2926       method_parameters_length,
2927       generic_signature_index,
2928       runtime_visible_annotations_length +
2929            runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
2930       runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length +
2931            runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
2932       runtime_visible_type_annotations_length +
2933            runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
2934       annotation_default_length,
2935       0);
2936 
2937   Method* const m = Method::allocate(_loader_data,
2938                                      code_length,
2939                                      access_flags,
2940                                      &sizes,
2941                                      ConstMethod::NORMAL,
2942                                      CHECK_NULL);
2943 
2944   ClassLoadingService::add_class_method_size(m->size()*wordSize);
2945 
2946   // Fill in information from fixed part (access_flags already set)
2947   m->set_constants(_cp);
2948   m->set_name_index(name_index);
2949   m->set_signature_index(signature_index);
2950   m->compute_from_signature(cp->symbol_at(signature_index));
2951   assert(args_size < 0 || args_size == m->size_of_parameters(), "");
2952 
2953   // Fill in code attribute information
2954   m->set_max_stack(max_stack);
2955   m->set_max_locals(max_locals);
2956   if (stackmap_data != NULL) {
2957     m->constMethod()->copy_stackmap_data(_loader_data,
2958                                          (u1*)stackmap_data,
2959                                          stackmap_data_length,
2960                                          CHECK_NULL);
2961   }
2962 
2963   // Copy byte codes
2964   m->set_code((u1*)code_start);
2965 
2966   // Copy line number table
2967   if (linenumber_table != NULL) {
2968     memcpy(m->compressed_linenumber_table(),
2969            linenumber_table->buffer(),
2970            linenumber_table_length);
2971   }
2972 
2973   // Copy exception table
2974   if (exception_table_length > 0) {
2975     Copy::conjoint_swap_if_needed<Endian::JAVA>(exception_table_start,
2976                                                 m->exception_table_start(),
2977                                                 exception_table_length * sizeof(ExceptionTableElement),
2978                                                 sizeof(u2));
2979   }
2980 
2981   // Copy method parameters
2982   if (method_parameters_length > 0) {
2983     MethodParametersElement* elem = m->constMethod()->method_parameters_start();
2984     for (int i = 0; i < method_parameters_length; i++) {
2985       elem[i].name_cp_index = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)method_parameters_data);
2986       method_parameters_data += 2;
2987       elem[i].flags = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)method_parameters_data);
2988       method_parameters_data += 2;
2989     }
2990   }
2991 
2992   // Copy checked exceptions
2993   if (checked_exceptions_length > 0) {
2994     Copy::conjoint_swap_if_needed<Endian::JAVA>(checked_exceptions_start,
2995                                                 m->checked_exceptions_start(),
2996                                                 checked_exceptions_length * sizeof(CheckedExceptionElement),
2997                                                 sizeof(u2));
2998   }
2999 
3000   // Copy class file LVT's/LVTT's into the HotSpot internal LVT.
3001   if (total_lvt_length > 0) {
3002     promoted_flags->set_has_localvariable_table();
3003     copy_localvariable_table(m->constMethod(),
3004                              lvt_cnt,
3005                              localvariable_table_length,
3006                              localvariable_table_start,
3007                              lvtt_cnt,
3008                              localvariable_type_table_length,
3009                              localvariable_type_table_start,
3010                              CHECK_NULL);
3011   }
3012 
3013   if (parsed_annotations.has_any_annotations())
3014     parsed_annotations.apply_to(methodHandle(THREAD, m));
3015 
3016   if (is_hidden()) { // Mark methods in hidden classes as 'hidden'.
3017     m->set_hidden(true);
3018   }
3019 
3020   // Copy annotations
3021   copy_method_annotations(m->constMethod(),
3022                           runtime_visible_annotations,
3023                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3024                           runtime_invisible_annotations,
3025                           runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3026                           runtime_visible_parameter_annotations,
3027                           runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length,
3028                           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations,
3029                           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
3030                           runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3031                           runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3032                           runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3033                           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3034                           annotation_default,
3035                           annotation_default_length,
3036                           CHECK_NULL);
3037 
3038   if (name == vmSymbols::finalize_method_name() &&
3039       signature == vmSymbols::void_method_signature()) {
3040     if (m->is_empty_method()) {
3041       _has_empty_finalizer = true;
3042     } else {
3043       _has_finalizer = true;
3044     }
3045   }
3046   if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name() &&
3047       signature == vmSymbols::void_method_signature() &&
3048       m->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
3049     _has_vanilla_constructor = true;
3050   }
3051 
3052   NOT_PRODUCT(m->verify());
3053   return m;
3054 }
3055 
3056 
3057 // The promoted_flags parameter is used to pass relevant access_flags
3058 // from the methods back up to the containing klass. These flag values
3059 // are added to klass's access_flags.
3060 // Side-effects: populates the _methods field in the parser
3061 void ClassFileParser::parse_methods(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3062                                     bool is_interface,
3063                                     bool is_inline_type,
3064                                     AccessFlags* promoted_flags,
3065                                     bool* has_final_method,
3066                                     bool* declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
3067                                     TRAPS) {
3068   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3069   assert(promoted_flags != NULL, "invariant");
3070   assert(has_final_method != NULL, "invariant");
3071   assert(declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods != NULL, "invariant");
3072 
3073   assert(NULL == _methods, "invariant");
3074 
3075   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // length
3076   const u2 length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3077   if (length == 0) {
3078     _methods = Universe::the_empty_method_array();
3079   } else {
3080     _methods = MetadataFactory::new_array<Method*>(_loader_data,
3081                                                    length,
3082                                                    NULL,
3083                                                    CHECK);
3084 
3085     for (int index = 0; index < length; index++) {
3086       Method* method = parse_method(cfs,
3087                                     is_interface,
3088                                     is_inline_type,
3089                                     _cp,
3090                                     promoted_flags,
3091                                     CHECK);
3092 
3093       if (method->is_final()) {
3094         *has_final_method = true;
3095       }
3096       // declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods: declares concrete instance methods, any access flags
3097       // used for interface initialization, and default method inheritance analysis
3098       if (is_interface && !(*declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods)
3099         && !method->is_abstract() && !method->is_static()) {
3100         *declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
3101       }
3102       _methods->at_put(index, method);
3103     }
3104 
3105     if (_need_verify && length > 1) {
3106       // Check duplicated methods
3107       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
3108       NameSigHash** names_and_sigs = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
3109         THREAD, NameSigHash*, HASH_ROW_SIZE);
3110       initialize_hashtable(names_and_sigs);
3111       bool dup = false;
3112       const Symbol* name = NULL;
3113       const Symbol* sig = NULL;
3114       {
3115         debug_only(NoSafepointVerifier nsv;)
3116         for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
3117           const Method* const m = _methods->at(i);
3118           name = m->name();
3119           sig = m->signature();
3120           // If no duplicates, add name/signature in hashtable names_and_sigs.
3121           if (!put_after_lookup(name, sig, names_and_sigs)) {
3122             dup = true;
3123             break;
3124           }
3125         }
3126       }
3127       if (dup) {
3128         classfile_parse_error("Duplicate method name \"%s\" with signature \"%s\" in class file %s",
3129                                name->as_C_string(), sig->as_klass_external_name(), CHECK);
3130       }
3131     }
3132   }
3133 }
3134 
3135 static const intArray* sort_methods(Array<Method*>* methods) {
3136   const int length = methods->length();
3137   // If JVMTI original method ordering or sharing is enabled we have to
3138   // remember the original class file ordering.
3139   // We temporarily use the vtable_index field in the Method* to store the
3140   // class file index, so we can read in after calling qsort.
3141   // Put the method ordering in the shared archive.
3142   if (JvmtiExport::can_maintain_original_method_order() || Arguments::is_dumping_archive()) {
3143     for (int index = 0; index < length; index++) {
3144       Method* const m = methods->at(index);
3145       assert(!m->valid_vtable_index(), "vtable index should not be set");
3146       m->set_vtable_index(index);
3147     }
3148   }
3149   // Sort method array by ascending method name (for faster lookups & vtable construction)
3150   // Note that the ordering is not alphabetical, see Symbol::fast_compare
3151   Method::sort_methods(methods);
3152 
3153   intArray* method_ordering = NULL;
3154   // If JVMTI original method ordering or sharing is enabled construct int
3155   // array remembering the original ordering
3156   if (JvmtiExport::can_maintain_original_method_order() || Arguments::is_dumping_archive()) {
3157     method_ordering = new intArray(length, length, -1);
3158     for (int index = 0; index < length; index++) {
3159       Method* const m = methods->at(index);
3160       const int old_index = m->vtable_index();
3161       assert(old_index >= 0 && old_index < length, "invalid method index");
3162       method_ordering->at_put(index, old_index);
3163       m->set_vtable_index(Method::invalid_vtable_index);
3164     }
3165   }
3166   return method_ordering;
3167 }
3168 
3169 // Parse generic_signature attribute for methods and fields
3170 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_generic_signature_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3171                                                       TRAPS) {
3172   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3173 
3174   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // generic_signature_index
3175   const u2 generic_signature_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3176   check_property(
3177     valid_symbol_at(generic_signature_index),
3178     "Invalid Signature attribute at constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3179     generic_signature_index, CHECK_0);
3180   return generic_signature_index;
3181 }

3183 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_sourcefile_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3184                                                            TRAPS) {
3185 
3186   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3187 
3188   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // sourcefile_index
3189   const u2 sourcefile_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3190   check_property(
3191     valid_symbol_at(sourcefile_index),
3192     "Invalid SourceFile attribute at constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3193     sourcefile_index, CHECK);
3194   set_class_sourcefile_index(sourcefile_index);
3195 }
3196 
3197 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_source_debug_extension_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3198                                                                        int length,
3199                                                                        TRAPS) {
3200   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3201 
3202   const u1* const sde_buffer = cfs->current();
3203   assert(sde_buffer != NULL, "null sde buffer");
3204 
3205   // Don't bother storing it if there is no way to retrieve it
3206   if (JvmtiExport::can_get_source_debug_extension()) {
3207     assert((length+1) > length, "Overflow checking");
3208     u1* const sde = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, u1, length+1);
3209     for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
3210       sde[i] = sde_buffer[i];
3211     }
3212     sde[length] = '\0';
3213     set_class_sde_buffer((const char*)sde, length);
3214   }
3215   // Got utf8 string, set stream position forward
3216   cfs->skip_u1(length, CHECK);
3217 }
3218 
3219 
3220 // Inner classes can be static, private or protected (classic VM does this)
3221 #define RECOGNIZED_INNER_CLASS_MODIFIERS ( JVM_RECOGNIZED_CLASS_MODIFIERS | \
3222                                            JVM_ACC_PRIVATE |                \
3223                                            JVM_ACC_PROTECTED |              \
3224                                            JVM_ACC_STATIC                   \
3225                                          )
3226 
3227 // Return number of classes in the inner classes attribute table
3228 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_inner_classes_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3229                                                             const u1* const inner_classes_attribute_start,
3230                                                             bool parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute,
3231                                                             u2 enclosing_method_class_index,
3232                                                             u2 enclosing_method_method_index,
3233                                                             TRAPS) {
3234   const u1* const current_mark = cfs->current();
3235   u2 length = 0;
3236   if (inner_classes_attribute_start != NULL) {
3237     cfs->set_current(inner_classes_attribute_start);
3238     cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // length
3239     length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3240   }
3241 
3242   // 4-tuples of shorts of inner classes data and 2 shorts of enclosing
3243   // method data:
3244   //   [inner_class_info_index,
3245   //    outer_class_info_index,
3246   //    inner_name_index,
3247   //    inner_class_access_flags,
3248   //    ...
3249   //    enclosing_method_class_index,
3250   //    enclosing_method_method_index]
3251   const int size = length * 4 + (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute ? 2 : 0);
3252   Array<u2>* const inner_classes = MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, size, CHECK_0);
3253   _inner_classes = inner_classes;
3254 
3255   int index = 0;
3256   cfs->guarantee_more(8 * length, CHECK_0);  // 4-tuples of u2
3257   for (int n = 0; n < length; n++) {
3258     // Inner class index
3259     const u2 inner_class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3260     check_property(
3261       valid_klass_reference_at(inner_class_info_index),
3262       "inner_class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3263       inner_class_info_index, CHECK_0);
3264     // Outer class index
3265     const u2 outer_class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3266     check_property(
3267       outer_class_info_index == 0 ||
3268         valid_klass_reference_at(outer_class_info_index),
3269       "outer_class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3270       outer_class_info_index, CHECK_0);
3271     // Inner class name
3272     const u2 inner_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3273     check_property(
3274       inner_name_index == 0 || valid_symbol_at(inner_name_index),
3275       "inner_name_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3276       inner_name_index, CHECK_0);
3277     if (_need_verify) {
3278       guarantee_property(inner_class_info_index != outer_class_info_index,
3279                          "Class is both outer and inner class in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3280     }
3281 
3282     jint recognized_modifiers = RECOGNIZED_INNER_CLASS_MODIFIERS;
3283     // JVM_ACC_MODULE is defined in JDK-9 and later.
3284     if (_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION) {
3285       recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_MODULE;
3286     }
3287     // JVM_ACC_VALUE is defined for class file version 55 and later
3288     if (supports_inline_types()) {
3289       recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_VALUE;
3290     }
3291 
3292     // Access flags
3293     jint flags = cfs->get_u2_fast() & recognized_modifiers;
3294 
3295     if ((flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE) && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
3296       // Set abstract bit for old class files for backward compatibility
3297       flags |= JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT;
3298     }
3299     verify_legal_class_modifiers(flags, CHECK_0);
3300     AccessFlags inner_access_flags(flags);
3301 
3302     inner_classes->at_put(index++, inner_class_info_index);
3303     inner_classes->at_put(index++, outer_class_info_index);
3304     inner_classes->at_put(index++, inner_name_index);
3305     inner_classes->at_put(index++, inner_access_flags.as_short());
3306   }
3307 
3308   // 4347400: make sure there's no duplicate entry in the classes array
3309   if (_need_verify && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3310     for(int i = 0; i < length * 4; i += 4) {
3311       for(int j = i + 4; j < length * 4; j += 4) {
3312         guarantee_property((inner_classes->at(i)   != inner_classes->at(j) ||
3313                             inner_classes->at(i+1) != inner_classes->at(j+1) ||
3314                             inner_classes->at(i+2) != inner_classes->at(j+2) ||
3315                             inner_classes->at(i+3) != inner_classes->at(j+3)),
3316                             "Duplicate entry in InnerClasses in class file %s",
3317                             CHECK_0);
3318       }
3319     }
3320   }
3321 
3322   // Set EnclosingMethod class and method indexes.
3323   if (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3324     inner_classes->at_put(index++, enclosing_method_class_index);
3325     inner_classes->at_put(index++, enclosing_method_method_index);
3326   }
3327   assert(index == size, "wrong size");
3328 
3329   // Restore buffer's current position.
3330   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3331 
3332   return length;
3333 }
3334 
3335 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_nest_members_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3336                                                            const u1* const nest_members_attribute_start,
3337                                                            TRAPS) {
3338   const u1* const current_mark = cfs->current();
3339   u2 length = 0;
3340   if (nest_members_attribute_start != NULL) {
3341     cfs->set_current(nest_members_attribute_start);
3342     cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // length
3343     length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3344   }
3345   const int size = length;
3346   Array<u2>* const nest_members = MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, size, CHECK_0);
3347   _nest_members = nest_members;
3348 
3349   int index = 0;
3350   cfs->guarantee_more(2 * length, CHECK_0);
3351   for (int n = 0; n < length; n++) {
3352     const u2 class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3353     check_property(
3354       valid_klass_reference_at(class_info_index),
3355       "Nest member class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3356       class_info_index, CHECK_0);
3357     nest_members->at_put(index++, class_info_index);
3358   }
3359   assert(index == size, "wrong size");
3360 
3361   // Restore buffer's current position.
3362   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3363 
3364   return length;
3365 }
3366 
3367 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_permitted_subclasses_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3368                                                                    const u1* const permitted_subclasses_attribute_start,
3369                                                                    TRAPS) {
3370   const u1* const current_mark = cfs->current();
3371   u2 length = 0;
3372   if (permitted_subclasses_attribute_start != NULL) {
3373     cfs->set_current(permitted_subclasses_attribute_start);
3374     cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // length
3375     length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3376   }
3377   if (length < 1) {
3378     classfile_parse_error("PermittedSubclasses attribute is empty in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3379   }
3380   const int size = length;
3381   Array<u2>* const permitted_subclasses = MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, size, CHECK_0);
3382   _permitted_subclasses = permitted_subclasses;
3383 
3384   int index = 0;
3385   cfs->guarantee_more(2 * length, CHECK_0);
3386   for (int n = 0; n < length; n++) {
3387     const u2 class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3388     check_property(
3389       valid_klass_reference_at(class_info_index),
3390       "Permitted subclass class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3391       class_info_index, CHECK_0);
3392     permitted_subclasses->at_put(index++, class_info_index);
3393   }
3394   assert(index == size, "wrong size");
3395 
3396   // Restore buffer's current position.
3397   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3398 
3399   return length;
3400 }
3401 
3402 //  Record {
3403 //    u2 attribute_name_index;
3404 //    u4 attribute_length;
3405 //    u2 components_count;
3406 //    component_info components[components_count];
3407 //  }
3408 //  component_info {
3409 //    u2 name_index;
3410 //    u2 descriptor_index
3411 //    u2 attributes_count;
3412 //    attribute_info_attributes[attributes_count];
3413 //  }
3414 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_record_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3415                                                      const ConstantPool* cp,
3416                                                      const u1* const record_attribute_start,
3417                                                      TRAPS) {
3418   const u1* const current_mark = cfs->current();
3419   int components_count = 0;
3420   unsigned int calculate_attr_size = 0;
3421   if (record_attribute_start != NULL) {
3422     cfs->set_current(record_attribute_start);
3423     cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // num of components
3424     components_count = (int)cfs->get_u2_fast();
3425     calculate_attr_size = 2;
3426   }
3427 
3428   Array<RecordComponent*>* const record_components =
3429     MetadataFactory::new_array<RecordComponent*>(_loader_data, components_count, NULL, CHECK_0);
3430   _record_components = record_components;
3431 
3432   for (int x = 0; x < components_count; x++) {
3433     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_0); // name_index, descriptor_index, attributes_count
3434 
3435     const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3436     check_property(valid_symbol_at(name_index),
3437       "Invalid constant pool index %u for name in Record attribute in class file %s",
3438       name_index, CHECK_0);
3439     const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_index);
3440     verify_legal_field_name(name, CHECK_0);
3441 
3442     const u2 descriptor_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3443     check_property(valid_symbol_at(descriptor_index),
3444       "Invalid constant pool index %u for descriptor in Record attribute in class file %s",
3445       descriptor_index, CHECK_0);
3446     const Symbol* const descr = cp->symbol_at(descriptor_index);
3447     verify_legal_field_signature(name, descr, CHECK_0);
3448 
3449     const u2 attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3450     calculate_attr_size += 6;
3451     u2 generic_sig_index = 0;
3452     const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
3453     int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
3454     const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
3455     int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
3456     bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
3457     const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
3458     int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3459     const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
3460     int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3461     bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
3462 
3463     // Expected attributes for record components are Signature, Runtime(In)VisibleAnnotations,
3464     // and Runtime(In)VisibleTypeAnnotations.  Other attributes are ignored.
3465     for (int y = 0; y < attributes_count; y++) {
3466       cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_0);  // attribute_name_index, attribute_length
3467       const u2 attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3468       const u4 attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
3469       calculate_attr_size += 6;
3470       check_property(
3471         valid_symbol_at(attribute_name_index),
3472         "Invalid Record attribute name index %u in class file %s",
3473         attribute_name_index, CHECK_0);
3474 
3475       const Symbol* const attribute_name = cp->symbol_at(attribute_name_index);
3476       if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
3477         if (generic_sig_index != 0) {
3478           classfile_parse_error(
3479             "Multiple Signature attributes for Record component in class file %s",
3480             CHECK_0);
3481         }
3482         if (attribute_length != 2) {
3483           classfile_parse_error(
3484             "Invalid Signature attribute length %u in Record component in class file %s",
