3485             attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3486         }
3487         generic_sig_index = parse_generic_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK_0);
3488 
3489       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
3490         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
3491           classfile_parse_error(
3492             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3493         }
3494         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3495         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
3496 
3497         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible annotation");
3498         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3499         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3500 
3501       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3502         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3503           classfile_parse_error(
3504             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3505         }
3506         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3507         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3508           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3509           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3510           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible annotation");
3511         }
3512         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3513 
3514       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3515         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3516           classfile_parse_error(
3517             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3518         }
3519         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3520         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3521 
3522         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible type annotation");
3523         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3524         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length);
3525 
3526       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3527         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3528           classfile_parse_error(
3529             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3530         }
3531         runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3532         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3533           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3534           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3535           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible type annotation");
3536         }
3537         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3538 
3539       } else {
3540         // Skip unknown attributes
3541         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3542       }
3543       calculate_attr_size += attribute_length;
3544     } // End of attributes For loop
3545 
3546     AnnotationArray* annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3547                                                         runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3548                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations,
3549                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3550                                                         CHECK_0);
3551     AnnotationArray* type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3552                                                              runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3553                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3554                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3555                                                              CHECK_0);
3556 
3557     RecordComponent* record_component =
3558       RecordComponent::allocate(_loader_data, name_index, descriptor_index,
3559                                 attributes_count, generic_sig_index,
3560                                 annotations, type_annotations, CHECK_0);
3561     record_components->at_put(x, record_component);
3562   }  // End of component processing loop
3563 
3564   // Restore buffer's current position.
3565   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3566   return calculate_attr_size;
3567 }
3568 
3569 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(TRAPS) {
3570   set_class_synthetic_flag(true);
3571 }
3572 
3573 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_signature_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs, TRAPS) {
3574   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3575 
3576   const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2(CHECK);
3577   check_property(
3578     valid_symbol_at(signature_index),
3579     "Invalid constant pool index %u in Signature attribute in class file %s",
3580     signature_index, CHECK);
3581   set_class_generic_signature_index(signature_index);
3582 }
3583 
3584 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3585                                                                   ConstantPool* cp,
3586                                                                   u4 attribute_byte_length,
3587                                                                   TRAPS) {
3588   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3589   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3590 
3591   const u1* const current_start = cfs->current();
3592 
3593   guarantee_property(attribute_byte_length >= sizeof(u2),
3594                      "Invalid BootstrapMethods attribute length %u in class file %s",
3595                      attribute_byte_length,
3596                      CHECK);
3597 
3598   cfs->guarantee_more(attribute_byte_length, CHECK);
3599 
3600   const int attribute_array_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3601 
3602   guarantee_property(_max_bootstrap_specifier_index < attribute_array_length,
3603                      "Short length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3604                      CHECK);
3605 
3606 
3607   // The attribute contains a counted array of counted tuples of shorts,
3608   // represending bootstrap specifiers:
3609   //    length*{bootstrap_method_index, argument_count*{argument_index}}
3610   const int operand_count = (attribute_byte_length - sizeof(u2)) / sizeof(u2);
3611   // operand_count = number of shorts in attr, except for leading length
3612 
3613   // The attribute is copied into a short[] array.
3614   // The array begins with a series of short[2] pairs, one for each tuple.
3615   const int index_size = (attribute_array_length * 2);
3616 
3617   Array<u2>* const operands =
3618     MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, index_size + operand_count, CHECK);
3619 
3620   // Eagerly assign operands so they will be deallocated with the constant
3621   // pool if there is an error.
3622   cp->set_operands(operands);
3623 
3624   int operand_fill_index = index_size;
3625   const int cp_size = cp->length();
3626 
3627   for (int n = 0; n < attribute_array_length; n++) {
3628     // Store a 32-bit offset into the header of the operand array.
3629     ConstantPool::operand_offset_at_put(operands, n, operand_fill_index);
3630 
3631     // Read a bootstrap specifier.
3632     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * 2, CHECK);  // bsm, argc
3633     const u2 bootstrap_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3634     const u2 argument_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3635     check_property(
3636       valid_cp_range(bootstrap_method_index, cp_size) &&
3637       cp->tag_at(bootstrap_method_index).is_method_handle(),
3638       "bootstrap_method_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3639       bootstrap_method_index,
3640       CHECK);
3641 
3642     guarantee_property((operand_fill_index + 1 + argument_count) < operands->length(),
3643       "Invalid BootstrapMethods num_bootstrap_methods or num_bootstrap_arguments value in class file %s",
3644       CHECK);
3645 
3646     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, bootstrap_method_index);
3647     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_count);
3648 
3649     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * argument_count, CHECK);  // argv[argc]
3650     for (int j = 0; j < argument_count; j++) {
3651       const u2 argument_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3652       check_property(
3653         valid_cp_range(argument_index, cp_size) &&
3654         cp->tag_at(argument_index).is_loadable_constant(),
3655         "argument_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3656         argument_index,
3657         CHECK);
3658       operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_index);
3659     }
3660   }
3661   guarantee_property(current_start + attribute_byte_length == cfs->current(),
3662                      "Bad length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3663                      CHECK);
3664 }
3665 
3666 bool ClassFileParser::supports_sealed_types() {
3667   return _major_version == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
3668          _minor_version == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
3669          Arguments::enable_preview();
3670 }
3671 
3672 bool ClassFileParser::supports_records() {
3673   return _major_version == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
3674          _minor_version == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
3675          Arguments::enable_preview();
3676 }
3677 
3678 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_attributes(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3679                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
3680                  ClassFileParser::ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
3681                                                  TRAPS) {
3682   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3683   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3684   assert(parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
3685 
3686   // Set inner classes attribute to default sentinel
3687   _inner_classes = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3688   // Set nest members attribute to default sentinel
3689   _nest_members = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3690   // Set _permitted_subclasses attribute to default sentinel
3691   _permitted_subclasses = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3692   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // attributes_count
3693   u2 attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3694   bool parsed_sourcefile_attribute = false;
3695   bool parsed_innerclasses_attribute = false;
3696   bool parsed_nest_members_attribute = false;
3697   bool parsed_permitted_subclasses_attribute = false;
3698   bool parsed_nest_host_attribute = false;
3699   bool parsed_record_attribute = false;
3700   bool parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = false;
3701   bool parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = false;
3702   const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
3703   int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
3704   const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
3705   int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
3706   const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
3707   int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3708   const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
3709   int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3710   bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
3711   bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
3712   bool parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = false;
3713   const u1* inner_classes_attribute_start = NULL;
3714   u4  inner_classes_attribute_length = 0;
3715   u2  enclosing_method_class_index = 0;
3716   u2  enclosing_method_method_index = 0;
3717   const u1* nest_members_attribute_start = NULL;
3718   u4  nest_members_attribute_length = 0;
3719   const u1* record_attribute_start = NULL;
3720   u4  record_attribute_length = 0;
3721   const u1* permitted_subclasses_attribute_start = NULL;
3722   u4  permitted_subclasses_attribute_length = 0;
3723 
3724   // Iterate over attributes
3725   while (attributes_count--) {
3726     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK);  // attribute_name_index, attribute_length
3727     const u2 attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3728     const u4 attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
3729     check_property(
3730       valid_symbol_at(attribute_name_index),
3731       "Attribute name has bad constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3732       attribute_name_index, CHECK);
3733     const Symbol* const tag = cp->symbol_at(attribute_name_index);
3734     if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_file()) {
3735       // Check for SourceFile tag
3736       if (_need_verify) {
3737         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong SourceFile attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3738       }
3739       if (parsed_sourcefile_attribute) {
3740         classfile_parse_error("Multiple SourceFile attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3741       } else {
3742         parsed_sourcefile_attribute = true;
3743       }
3744       parse_classfile_sourcefile_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3745     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_debug_extension()) {
3746       // Check for SourceDebugExtension tag
3747       if (parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist) {
3748           classfile_parse_error(
3749             "Multiple SourceDebugExtension attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3750       }
3751       parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = true;
3752       parse_classfile_source_debug_extension_attribute(cfs, (int)attribute_length, CHECK);
3753     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_inner_classes()) {
3754       // Check for InnerClasses tag
3755       if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute) {
3756         classfile_parse_error("Multiple InnerClasses attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3757       } else {
3758         parsed_innerclasses_attribute = true;
3759       }
3760       inner_classes_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3761       inner_classes_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3762       cfs->skip_u1(inner_classes_attribute_length, CHECK);
3763     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_synthetic()) {
3764       // Check for Synthetic tag
3765       // Shouldn't we check that the synthetic flags wasn't already set? - not required in spec
3766       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3767         classfile_parse_error(
3768           "Invalid Synthetic classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3769           attribute_length, CHECK);
3770       }
3771       parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(CHECK);
3772     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_deprecated()) {
3773       // Check for Deprecatd tag - 4276120
3774       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3775         classfile_parse_error(
3776           "Invalid Deprecated classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3777           attribute_length, CHECK);
3778       }
3779     } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3780       if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
3781         if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
3782           classfile_parse_error(
3783             "Multiple Signature attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3784         }
3785         if (attribute_length != 2) {
3786           classfile_parse_error(
3787             "Wrong Signature attribute length %u in class file %s",
3788             attribute_length, CHECK);
3789         }
3790         parse_classfile_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3791       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
3792         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
3793           classfile_parse_error(
3794             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3795         }
3796         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3797         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
3798         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null visible annotations");
3799         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK);
3800         parse_annotations(cp,
3801                           runtime_visible_annotations,
3802                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3803                           parsed_annotations,
3804                           _loader_data,
3805                           _can_access_vm_annotations,
3806                           CHECK);
3807         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3808       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3809         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3810           classfile_parse_error(
3811             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3812         }
3813         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3814         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3815           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3816           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3817           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null invisible annotations");
3818         }
3819         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3820       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_enclosing_method()) {
3821         if (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3822           classfile_parse_error("Multiple EnclosingMethod attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3823         } else {
3824           parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = true;
3825         }
3826         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 4,
3827           "Wrong EnclosingMethod attribute length %u in class file %s",
3828           attribute_length, CHECK);
3829         cfs->guarantee_more(4, CHECK);  // class_index, method_index
3830         enclosing_method_class_index  = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3831         enclosing_method_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3832         if (enclosing_method_class_index == 0) {
3833           classfile_parse_error("Invalid class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3834         }
3835         // Validate the constant pool indices and types
3836         check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(enclosing_method_class_index),
3837           "Invalid or out-of-bounds class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3838         if (enclosing_method_method_index != 0 &&
3839             (!cp->is_within_bounds(enclosing_method_method_index) ||
3840              !cp->tag_at(enclosing_method_method_index).is_name_and_type())) {
3841           classfile_parse_error("Invalid or out-of-bounds method index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3842         }
3843       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_bootstrap_methods() &&
3844                  _major_version >= Verifier::INVOKEDYNAMIC_MAJOR_VERSION) {
3845         if (parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute) {
3846           classfile_parse_error("Multiple BootstrapMethods attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3847         }
3848         parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = true;
3849         parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(cfs, cp, attribute_length, CHECK);
3850       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3851         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3852           classfile_parse_error(
3853             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3854         }
3855         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3856         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3857         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null visible type annotations");
3858         // No need for the VM to parse Type annotations
3859         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK);
3860       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3861         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3862           classfile_parse_error(
3863             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3864         } else {
3865           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3866         }
3867         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3868           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3869           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3870           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null invisible type annotations");
3871         }
3872         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3873       } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION) {
3874         if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_members()) {
3875           // Check for NestMembers tag
3876           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3877             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3878           } else {
3879             parsed_nest_members_attribute = true;
3880           }
3881           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3882             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestHost and NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3883           }
3884           nest_members_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3885           nest_members_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3886           cfs->skip_u1(nest_members_attribute_length, CHECK);
3887         } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_host()) {
3888           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3889             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3890           } else {
3891             parsed_nest_host_attribute = true;
3892           }
3893           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3894             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestMembers and NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3895           }
3896           if (_need_verify) {
3897             guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong NestHost attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3898           }
3899           cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);
3900           u2 class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3901           check_property(
3902                          valid_klass_reference_at(class_info_index),
3903                          "Nest-host class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3904                          class_info_index, CHECK);
3905           _nest_host = class_info_index;
3906         } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION) {
3907           if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_record()) {
3908             // Skip over Record attribute if not supported or if super class is
3909             // not java.lang.Record.
3910             if (supports_records() &&
3911                 cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index) == vmSymbols::java_lang_Record()) {
3912               if (parsed_record_attribute) {
3913                 classfile_parse_error("Multiple Record attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3914               }
3915               // Check that class is final and not abstract.
3916               if (!_access_flags.is_final() || _access_flags.is_abstract()) {
3917                 classfile_parse_error("Record attribute in non-final or abstract class file %s", CHECK);
3918               }
3919               parsed_record_attribute = true;
3920               record_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3921               record_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3922             } else if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, record)) {
3923               // Log why the Record attribute was ignored.  Note that if the
3924               // class file version is JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION.65535 and
3925               // --enable-preview wasn't specified then a java.lang.UnsupportedClassVersionError
3926               // exception would have been thrown.
3927               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
3928               if (supports_records()) {
3929                 log_info(class, record)(
3930                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because super type is not java.lang.Record",
3931                   _class_name->as_C_string());
3932               } else {
3933                 log_info(class, record)(
3934                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because class file version is not %d.65535",
3935                    _class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
3936               }
3937             }
3938             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3939           } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_15_VERSION) {
3940             // Check for PermittedSubclasses tag
3941             if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_permitted_subclasses()) {
3942               if (supports_sealed_types()) {
3943                 if (parsed_permitted_subclasses_attribute) {
3944                   classfile_parse_error("Multiple PermittedSubclasses attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3945                 }
3946                 // Classes marked ACC_FINAL cannot have a PermittedSubclasses attribute.
3947                 if (_access_flags.is_final()) {
3948                   classfile_parse_error("PermittedSubclasses attribute in final class file %s", CHECK);
3949                 }
3950                 parsed_permitted_subclasses_attribute = true;
3951                 permitted_subclasses_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3952                 permitted_subclasses_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3953               }
3954               cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3955             } else {
3956               // Unknown attribute
3957               cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3958             }
3959           } else {
3960             // Unknown attribute
3961             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3962           }
3963         } else {
3964           // Unknown attribute
3965           cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3966         }
3967       } else {
3968         // Unknown attribute
3969         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3970       }
3971     } else {
3972       // Unknown attribute
3973       cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3974     }
3975   }
3976   _class_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3977                                             runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3978                                             runtime_invisible_annotations,
3979                                             runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3980                                             CHECK);
3981   _class_type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3982                                                  runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3983                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3984                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3985                                                  CHECK);
3986 
3987   if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute || parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3988     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_inner_classes_attribute(
3989                             cfs,
3990                             inner_classes_attribute_start,
3991                             parsed_innerclasses_attribute,
3992                             enclosing_method_class_index,
3993                             enclosing_method_method_index,
3994                             CHECK);
3995     if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute && _need_verify && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3996       guarantee_property(
3997         inner_classes_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + 4 * sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
3998         "Wrong InnerClasses attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3999     }
4000   }
4001 
4002   if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
4003     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_nest_members_attribute(
4004                             cfs,
4005                             nest_members_attribute_start,
4006                             CHECK);
4007     if (_need_verify) {
4008       guarantee_property(
4009         nest_members_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
4010         "Wrong NestMembers attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
4011     }
4012   }
4013 
4014   if (parsed_record_attribute) {
4015     const unsigned int calculated_attr_length = parse_classfile_record_attribute(
4016                             cfs,
4017                             cp,
4018                             record_attribute_start,
4019                             CHECK);
4020     if (_need_verify) {
4021       guarantee_property(record_attribute_length == calculated_attr_length,
4022                          "Record attribute has wrong length in class file %s",
4023                          CHECK);
4024     }
4025   }
4026 
4027   if (parsed_permitted_subclasses_attribute) {
4028     const u2 num_subclasses = parse_classfile_permitted_subclasses_attribute(
4029                             cfs,
4030                             permitted_subclasses_attribute_start,
4031                             CHECK);
4032     if (_need_verify) {
4033       guarantee_property(
4034         permitted_subclasses_attribute_length == sizeof(num_subclasses) + sizeof(u2) * num_subclasses,
4035         "Wrong PermittedSubclasses attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
4036     }
4037   }
4038 
4039   if (_max_bootstrap_specifier_index >= 0) {
4040     guarantee_property(parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute,
4041                        "Missing BootstrapMethods attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
4042   }
4043 }
4044 
4045 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_attributes(InstanceKlass* k) {
4046   assert(k != NULL, "invariant");
4047 
4048   if (_synthetic_flag)
4049     k->set_is_synthetic();
4050   if (_sourcefile_index != 0) {
4051     k->set_source_file_name_index(_sourcefile_index);
4052   }
4053   if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
4054     k->set_generic_signature_index(_generic_signature_index);
4055   }
4056   if (_sde_buffer != NULL) {
4057     k->set_source_debug_extension(_sde_buffer, _sde_length);
4058   }
4059 }
4060 
4061 // Create the Annotations object that will
4062 // hold the annotations array for the Klass.
4063 void ClassFileParser::create_combined_annotations(TRAPS) {
4064     if (_class_annotations == NULL &&
4065         _class_type_annotations == NULL &&
4066         _fields_annotations == NULL &&
4067         _fields_type_annotations == NULL) {
4068       // Don't create the Annotations object unnecessarily.
4069       return;
4070     }
4071 
4072     Annotations* const annotations = Annotations::allocate(_loader_data, CHECK);
4073     annotations->set_class_annotations(_class_annotations);
4074     annotations->set_class_type_annotations(_class_type_annotations);
4075     annotations->set_fields_annotations(_fields_annotations);
4076     annotations->set_fields_type_annotations(_fields_type_annotations);
4077 
4078     // This is the Annotations object that will be
4079     // assigned to InstanceKlass being constructed.
4080     _combined_annotations = annotations;
4081 
4082     // The annotations arrays below has been transfered the
4083     // _combined_annotations so these fields can now be cleared.
4084     _class_annotations       = NULL;
4085     _class_type_annotations  = NULL;
4086     _fields_annotations      = NULL;
4087     _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
4088 }
4089 
4090 // Transfer ownership of metadata allocated to the InstanceKlass.
4091 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_metadata(
4092                                             InstanceKlass* this_klass,
4093                                             int java_fields_count,
4094                                             TRAPS) {
4095   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
4096 
4097   _cp->set_pool_holder(this_klass);
4098   this_klass->set_constants(_cp);
4099   this_klass->set_fields(_fields, java_fields_count);
4100   this_klass->set_methods(_methods);
4101   this_klass->set_inner_classes(_inner_classes);
4102   this_klass->set_nest_members(_nest_members);
4103   this_klass->set_nest_host_index(_nest_host);
4104   this_klass->set_annotations(_combined_annotations);
4105   this_klass->set_permitted_subclasses(_permitted_subclasses);
4106   this_klass->set_record_components(_record_components);
4107   // Delay the setting of _local_interfaces and _transitive_interfaces until after
4108   // initialize_supers() in fill_instance_klass(). It is because the _local_interfaces could
4109   // be shared with _transitive_interfaces and _transitive_interfaces may be shared with
4110   // its _super. If an OOM occurs while loading the current klass, its _super field
4111   // may not have been set. When GC tries to free the klass, the _transitive_interfaces
4112   // may be deallocated mistakenly in InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(). Subsequent
4113   // dereferences to the deallocated _transitive_interfaces will result in a crash.
4114 
4115   // Clear out these fields so they don't get deallocated by the destructor
4116   clear_class_metadata();
4117 }
4118 
4119 AnnotationArray* ClassFileParser::assemble_annotations(const u1* const runtime_visible_annotations,
4120                                                        int runtime_visible_annotations_length,
4121                                                        const u1* const runtime_invisible_annotations,
4122                                                        int runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4123                                                        TRAPS) {
4124   AnnotationArray* annotations = NULL;
4125   if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL ||
4126       runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4127     annotations = MetadataFactory::new_array<u1>(_loader_data,
4128                                           runtime_visible_annotations_length +
4129                                           runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4130                                           CHECK_(annotations));
4131     if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
4132       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_visible_annotations_length; i++) {
4133         annotations->at_put(i, runtime_visible_annotations[i]);
4134       }
4135     }
4136     if (runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4137       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_invisible_annotations_length; i++) {
4138         int append = runtime_visible_annotations_length+i;
4139         annotations->at_put(append, runtime_invisible_annotations[i]);
4140       }
4141     }
4142   }
4143   return annotations;
4144 }
4145 
4146 const InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::parse_super_class(ConstantPool* const cp,
4147                                                         const int super_class_index,
4148                                                         const bool need_verify,
4149                                                         TRAPS) {
4150   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4151   const InstanceKlass* super_klass = NULL;
4152 
4153   if (super_class_index == 0) {
4154     check_property(_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()
4155                    || (_access_flags.get_flags() & JVM_ACC_VALUE),
4156                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4157                    super_class_index,
4158                    CHECK_NULL);
4159   } else {
4160     check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(super_class_index),
4161                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4162                    super_class_index,
4163                    CHECK_NULL);
4164     // The class name should be legal because it is checked when parsing constant pool.
4165     // However, make sure it is not an array type.
4166     bool is_array = false;
4167     if (cp->tag_at(super_class_index).is_klass()) {
4168       super_klass = InstanceKlass::cast(cp->resolved_klass_at(super_class_index));
4169       if (need_verify)
4170         is_array = super_klass->is_array_klass();
4171     } else if (need_verify) {
4172       is_array = (cp->klass_name_at(super_class_index)->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY);
4173     }
4174     if (need_verify) {
4175       guarantee_property(!is_array,
4176                         "Bad superclass name in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
4177     }
4178   }
4179   return super_klass;
4180 }
4181 
4182 #ifndef PRODUCT
4183 static void print_field_layout(const Symbol* name,
4184                                Array<u2>* fields,
4185                                ConstantPool* cp,
4186                                int instance_size,
4187                                int instance_fields_start,
4188                                int instance_fields_end,
4189                                int static_fields_end) {
4190 
4191   assert(name != NULL, "invariant");
4192 
4193   tty->print("%s: field layout\n", name->as_klass_external_name());
4194   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_start, "--- instance fields start ---");
4195   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4196     if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4197       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4198         fs.offset(),
4199         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4200         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4201     }
4202   }
4203   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_end, "--- instance fields end ---");
4204   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_size * wordSize, "--- instance ends ---");
4205   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields(), "--- static fields start ---");
4206   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4207     if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4208       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4209         fs.offset(),
4210         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4211         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4212     }
4213   }
4214   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", static_fields_end, "--- static fields end ---");
4215   tty->print("\n");
4216 }
4217 #endif
4218 
4219 OopMapBlocksBuilder::OopMapBlocksBuilder(unsigned int max_blocks) {
4220   _max_nonstatic_oop_maps = max_blocks;
4221   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = 0;
4222   if (max_blocks == 0) {
4223     _nonstatic_oop_maps = NULL;
4224   } else {
4225     _nonstatic_oop_maps =
4226         NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4227     memset(_nonstatic_oop_maps, 0, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * max_blocks);
4228   }
4229 }
4230 
4231 OopMapBlock* OopMapBlocksBuilder::last_oop_map() const {
4232   assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0, "Has no oop maps");
4233   return _nonstatic_oop_maps + (_nonstatic_oop_map_count - 1);
4234 }
4235 
4236 // addition of super oop maps
4237 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::initialize_inherited_blocks(OopMapBlock* blocks, unsigned int nof_blocks) {
4238   assert(nof_blocks && _nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0 &&
4239          nof_blocks <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "invariant");
4240 
4241   memcpy(_nonstatic_oop_maps, blocks, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * nof_blocks);
4242   _nonstatic_oop_map_count += nof_blocks;
4243 }
4244 
4245 // collection of oops
4246 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::add(int offset, int count) {
4247   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0) {
4248     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4249   }
4250   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4251   if (nonstatic_oop_map->count() == 0) {  // Unused map, set it up
4252     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4253     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4254   } else if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(offset)) { // contiguous, add
4255     nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(count);
4256   } else { // Need a new one...
4257     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4258     assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "range check");
4259     nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4260     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4261     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4262   }
4263 }
4264 
4265 // general purpose copy, e.g. into allocated instanceKlass
4266 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::copy(OopMapBlock* dst) {
4267   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count != 0) {
4268     memcpy(dst, _nonstatic_oop_maps, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4269   }
4270 }
4271 
4272 // Sort and compact adjacent blocks
4273 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::compact() {
4274   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= 1) {
4275     return;
4276   }
4277   /*
4278    * Since field layout sneeks in oops before values, we will be able to condense
4279    * blocks. There is potential to compact between super, own refs and values
4280    * containing refs.
4281    *
4282    * Currently compaction is slightly limited due to values being 8 byte aligned.
4283    * This may well change: FixMe if it doesn't, the code below is fairly general purpose
4284    * and maybe it doesn't need to be.
4285    */
4286   qsort(_nonstatic_oop_maps, _nonstatic_oop_map_count, sizeof(OopMapBlock),
4287         (_sort_Fn)OopMapBlock::compare_offset);
4288   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count < 2) {
4289     return;
4290   }
4291 
4292   // Make a temp copy, and iterate through and copy back into the original
4293   ResourceMark rm;
4294   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy =
4295       NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4296   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy_end = oop_maps_copy + _nonstatic_oop_map_count;
4297   copy(oop_maps_copy);
4298   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4299   unsigned int new_count = 1;
4300   oop_maps_copy++;
4301   while(oop_maps_copy < oop_maps_copy_end) {
4302     assert(nonstatic_oop_map->offset() < oop_maps_copy->offset(), "invariant");
4303     if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(oop_maps_copy->offset())) {
4304       nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4305     } else {
4306       nonstatic_oop_map++;
4307       new_count++;
4308       nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(oop_maps_copy->offset());
4309       nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4310     }
4311     oop_maps_copy++;
4312   }
4313   assert(new_count <= _nonstatic_oop_map_count, "end up with more maps after compact() ?");
4314   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = new_count;
4315 }
4316 
4317 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_on(outputStream* st) const {
4318   st->print_cr("  OopMapBlocks: %3d  /%3d", _nonstatic_oop_map_count, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4319   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
4320     OopMapBlock* map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4321     OopMapBlock* last_map = last_oop_map();
4322     assert(map <= last_map, "Last less than first");
4323     while (map <= last_map) {
4324       st->print_cr("    Offset: %3d  -%3d Count: %3d", map->offset(),
4325                    map->offset() + map->offset_span() - heapOopSize, map->count());
4326       map++;
4327     }
4328   }
4329 }
4330 
4331 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_value_on(outputStream* st) const {
4332   print_on(st);
4333 }
4334 
4335 void ClassFileParser::throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_DECL,
4336                                                 const char* msg,
4337                                                 const Symbol* name,
4338                                                 const Symbol* sig) const {
4339 
4340   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
4341   if (name == NULL || sig == NULL) {
4342     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4343         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4344         "class: %s - %s", _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4345   }
4346   else {
4347     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4348         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4349         "\"%s\" sig: \"%s\" class: %s - %s", name->as_C_string(), sig->as_C_string(),
4350         _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4351   }
4352 }
4353 
4354 // Layout fields and fill in FieldLayoutInfo.  Could use more refactoring!
4355 void ClassFileParser::layout_fields(ConstantPool* cp,
4356                                     const FieldAllocationCount* fac,
4357                                     const ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
4358                                     FieldLayoutInfo* info,
4359                                     TRAPS) {
4360 
4361   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4362 
4363   // Field size and offset computation
4364   int nonstatic_field_size = _super_klass == NULL ? 0 :
4365                                _super_klass->nonstatic_field_size();
4366   int next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = 0;
4367   int first_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = 0;
4368 
4369   // Fields that are inline types are handled differently depending if they are static or not:
4370   // - static fields are oops
4371   // - non-static fields are embedded
4372 
4373   // Count the contended fields by type.
4374   //
4375   // We ignore static fields, because @Contended is not supported for them.
4376   // The layout code below will also ignore the static fields.
4377   int nonstatic_contended_count = 0;
4378   FieldAllocationCount fac_contended;
4379   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4380     FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4381     if (fs.is_contended()) {
4382       fac_contended.count[atype]++;
4383       if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4384         nonstatic_contended_count++;
4385       }
4386     }
4387   }
4388 
4389 
4390   // Calculate the starting byte offsets
4391   int next_static_oop_offset    = InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields();
4392   // Inline types in static fields are not embedded, they are handled with oops
4393   int next_static_double_offset = next_static_oop_offset +
4394                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + fac->count[STATIC_INLINE]) * heapOopSize);
4395   if (fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) {
4396     next_static_double_offset = align_up(next_static_double_offset, BytesPerLong);
4397   }
4398 
4399   int next_static_word_offset   = next_static_double_offset +
4400                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) * BytesPerLong);
4401   int next_static_short_offset  = next_static_word_offset +
4402                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_WORD]) * BytesPerInt);
4403   int next_static_byte_offset   = next_static_short_offset +
4404                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_SHORT]) * BytesPerShort);
4405 
4406   int nonstatic_fields_start  = instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() +
4407                                 nonstatic_field_size * heapOopSize;
4408 
4409   // First field of inline types is aligned on a long boundary in order to ease
4410   // in-lining of inline types (with header removal) in packed arrays and
4411   // inlined fields
4412   int initial_inline_type_padding = 0;
4413   if (is_inline_type()) {
4414     int old = nonstatic_fields_start;
4415     nonstatic_fields_start = align_up(nonstatic_fields_start, BytesPerLong);
4416     initial_inline_type_padding = nonstatic_fields_start - old;
4417   }
4418 
4419   int next_nonstatic_field_offset = nonstatic_fields_start;
4420 
4421   const bool is_contended_class     = parsed_annotations->is_contended();
4422 
4423   // Class is contended, pad before all the fields
4424   if (is_contended_class) {
4425     next_nonstatic_field_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4426   }
4427 
4428   // Temporary inline types restrictions
4429   if (is_inline_type()) {
4430     if (is_contended_class) {
4431       throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support @Contended annotation yet");
4432       return;
4433     }
4434   }
4435 
4436   // Compute the non-contended fields count.
4437   // The packing code below relies on these counts to determine if some field
4438   // can be squeezed into the alignment gap. Contended fields are obviously
4439   // exempt from that.
4440   unsigned int nonstatic_double_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE];
4441   unsigned int nonstatic_word_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_WORD];
4442   unsigned int nonstatic_short_count  = fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT]  - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_SHORT];
4443   unsigned int nonstatic_byte_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_BYTE];
4444   unsigned int nonstatic_oop_count    = fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP]    - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_OOP];
4445 
4446   int static_inline_type_count = 0;
4447   int nonstatic_inline_type_count = 0;
4448   int* nonstatic_inline_type_indexes = NULL;
4449   Klass** nonstatic_inline_type_klasses = NULL;
4450   unsigned int inline_type_oop_map_count = 0;
4451   int inline_types_not_inlined = 0;
4452   int not_atomic_inline_types = 0;
4453 
4454   int max_nonstatic_inline_type = fac->count[NONSTATIC_INLINE] + 1;
4455 
4456   nonstatic_inline_type_indexes = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, int,
4457                                                                max_nonstatic_inline_type);
4458   for (int i = 0; i < max_nonstatic_inline_type; i++) {
4459     nonstatic_inline_type_indexes[i] = -1;
4460   }
4461   nonstatic_inline_type_klasses = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, Klass*,
4462                                                                max_nonstatic_inline_type);
4463 
4464   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, _cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4465     if (fs.allocation_type() == STATIC_INLINE) {
4466       ResourceMark rm;
4467       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4468         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4469       }
4470       static_inline_type_count++;
4471     } else if (fs.allocation_type() == NONSTATIC_INLINE) {
4472       // Pre-resolve the inline field and check for inline type circularity issues.
4473       ResourceMark rm;
4474       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4475         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4476       }
4477       Klass* klass =
4478         SystemDictionary::resolve_inline_type_field_or_fail(&fs,
4479                                                             Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
4480                                                             _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
4481       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
4482       if (!klass->access_flags().is_inline_type()) {
4483         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError());
4484       }
4485       ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4486       // Conditions to apply flattening or not should be defined in a single place
4487       bool too_big_to_allocate_inline = (InlineFieldMaxFlatSize >= 0 &&
4488                                  (vk->size_helper() * HeapWordSize) > InlineFieldMaxFlatSize);
4489       bool too_atomic_to_allocate_inline = vk->is_declared_atomic();
4490       bool too_volatile_to_allocate_inline = fs.access_flags().is_volatile();
4491       if (vk->is_naturally_atomic()) {
4492         too_atomic_to_allocate_inline = false;
4493         // too_volatile_to_allocate_inline = false; //FIXME
4494         // volatile fields are currently never inlined, this could change in the future
4495       }
4496       if (!(too_big_to_allocate_inline | too_atomic_to_allocate_inline | too_volatile_to_allocate_inline)) {
4497         nonstatic_inline_type_indexes[nonstatic_inline_type_count] = fs.index();
4498         nonstatic_inline_type_klasses[nonstatic_inline_type_count] = klass;
4499         nonstatic_inline_type_count++;
4500 
4501         ValueKlass* vklass = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4502         if (vklass->contains_oops()) {
4503           inline_type_oop_map_count += vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4504         }
4505         fs.set_inlined(true);
4506         if (!vk->is_atomic()) {  // flat and non-atomic: take note
4507           not_atomic_inline_types++;
4508         }
4509       } else {
4510         inline_types_not_inlined++;
4511         fs.set_inlined(false);
4512       }
4513     }
4514   }
4515 
4516   // Adjusting non_static_oop_count to take into account inline types fields not inlined;
4517   nonstatic_oop_count += inline_types_not_inlined;
4518 
4519   // Total non-static fields count, including every contended field
4520   unsigned int nonstatic_fields_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD] +
4521                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE] +
4522                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_INLINE];
4523 
4524   const bool super_has_nonstatic_fields =
4525           (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_nonstatic_fields());
4526   const bool has_nonstatic_fields =
4527     super_has_nonstatic_fields || (nonstatic_fields_count != 0);
4528   const bool has_nonstatic_inline_fields = nonstatic_inline_type_count > 0;
4529 
4530   if (is_inline_type() && (!has_nonstatic_fields)) {
4531     // There are a number of fixes required throughout the type system and JIT
4532     throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support zero instance size yet");
4533     return;
4534   }
4535 
4536   // Prepare list of oops for oop map generation.
4537   //
4538   // "offset" and "count" lists are describing the set of contiguous oop
4539   // regions. offset[i] is the start of the i-th region, which then has
4540   // count[i] oops following. Before we know how many regions are required,
4541   // we pessimistically allocate the maps to fit all the oops into the
4542   // distinct regions.
4543   //
4544   int super_oop_map_count = (_super_klass == NULL) ? 0 :_super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4545   int max_oop_map_count =
4546       super_oop_map_count +
4547       fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] +
4548       inline_type_oop_map_count +
4549       inline_types_not_inlined;
4550 
4551   OopMapBlocksBuilder* nonstatic_oop_maps = new OopMapBlocksBuilder(max_oop_map_count);
4552   if (super_oop_map_count > 0) {
4553     nonstatic_oop_maps->initialize_inherited_blocks(_super_klass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps(),
4554                                                     _super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count());
4555   }
4556 
4557   int first_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0; // will be set for first oop field
4558 
4559   bool compact_fields  = true;
4560   bool allocate_oops_first = false;
4561 
4562   int next_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0;
4563   int next_nonstatic_double_offset = 0;
4564 
4565   // Rearrange fields for a given allocation style
4566   if (allocate_oops_first) {
4567     // Fields order: oops, longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, padded fields
4568     next_nonstatic_oop_offset    = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4569     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset +
4570                                     (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4571   } else {
4572     // Fields order: longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, oops, padded fields
4573     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4574   }
4575 
4576   int nonstatic_oop_space_count   = 0;
4577   int nonstatic_word_space_count  = 0;
4578   int nonstatic_short_space_count = 0;
4579   int nonstatic_byte_space_count  = 0;
4580   int nonstatic_oop_space_offset = 0;
4581   int nonstatic_word_space_offset = 0;
4582   int nonstatic_short_space_offset = 0;
4583   int nonstatic_byte_space_offset = 0;
4584 
4585   // Try to squeeze some of the fields into the gaps due to
4586   // long/double alignment.
4587   if (nonstatic_double_count > 0) {
4588     int offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4589     next_nonstatic_double_offset = align_up(offset, BytesPerLong);
4590     if (compact_fields && offset != next_nonstatic_double_offset) {
4591       // Allocate available fields into the gap before double field.
4592       int length = next_nonstatic_double_offset - offset;
4593       assert(length == BytesPerInt, "");
4594       nonstatic_word_space_offset = offset;
4595       if (nonstatic_word_count > 0) {
4596         nonstatic_word_count      -= 1;
4597         nonstatic_word_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4598         length -= BytesPerInt;
4599         offset += BytesPerInt;
4600       }
4601       nonstatic_short_space_offset = offset;
4602       while (length >= BytesPerShort && nonstatic_short_count > 0) {
4603         nonstatic_short_count       -= 1;
4604         nonstatic_short_space_count += 1;
4605         length -= BytesPerShort;
4606         offset += BytesPerShort;
4607       }
4608       nonstatic_byte_space_offset = offset;
4609       while (length > 0 && nonstatic_byte_count > 0) {
4610         nonstatic_byte_count       -= 1;
4611         nonstatic_byte_space_count += 1;
4612         length -= 1;
4613       }
4614       // Allocate oop field in the gap if there are no other fields for that.
4615       nonstatic_oop_space_offset = offset;
4616       if (length >= heapOopSize && nonstatic_oop_count > 0 &&
4617           !allocate_oops_first) { // when oop fields not first
4618         nonstatic_oop_count      -= 1;
4619         nonstatic_oop_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4620         length -= heapOopSize;
4621         offset += heapOopSize;
4622       }
4623     }
4624   }
4625 
4626   int next_nonstatic_word_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset +
4627                                      (nonstatic_double_count * BytesPerLong);
4628   int next_nonstatic_short_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset +
4629                                       (nonstatic_word_count * BytesPerInt);
4630   int next_nonstatic_byte_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset +
4631                                      (nonstatic_short_count * BytesPerShort);
4632   int next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset +
4633                                        nonstatic_byte_count;
4634 
4635   // let oops jump before padding with this allocation style
4636   if (!allocate_oops_first) {
4637     next_nonstatic_oop_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4638     if( nonstatic_oop_count > 0 ) {
4639       next_nonstatic_oop_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_oop_offset, heapOopSize);
4640     }
4641     next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset + (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4642   }
4643 
4644   // Aligning embedded inline types
4645   // bug below, the current algorithm to layout embedded inline types always put them at the
4646   // end of the layout, which doesn't match the different allocation policies the VM is
4647   // supposed to provide => FixMe
4648   // Note also that the current alignment policy is to make each inline type starting on a
4649   // 64 bits boundary. This could be optimized later. For instance, it could be nice to
4650   // align inline types according to their most constrained internal type.
4651   next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4652   int next_inline_type_index = 0;
4653 
4654   // Iterate over fields again and compute correct offsets.
4655   // The field allocation type was temporarily stored in the offset slot.
4656   // oop fields are located before non-oop fields (static and non-static).
4657   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4658 
4659     // skip already laid out fields
4660     if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4661 
4662     // contended instance fields are handled below
4663     if (fs.is_contended() && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4664 
4665     int real_offset = 0;
4666     const FieldAllocationType atype = (const FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4667 
4668     // pack the rest of the fields
4669     switch (atype) {
4670       // Inline types in static fields are handled with oops
4671       case STATIC_INLINE:   // Fallthrough
4672       case STATIC_OOP:
4673         real_offset = next_static_oop_offset;
4674         next_static_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4675         break;
4676       case STATIC_BYTE:
4677         real_offset = next_static_byte_offset;
4678         next_static_byte_offset += 1;
4679         break;
4680       case STATIC_SHORT:
4681         real_offset = next_static_short_offset;
4682         next_static_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4683         break;
4684       case STATIC_WORD:
4685         real_offset = next_static_word_offset;
4686         next_static_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4687         break;
4688       case STATIC_DOUBLE:
4689         real_offset = next_static_double_offset;
4690         next_static_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4691         break;
4692       case NONSTATIC_INLINE:
4693         if (fs.is_inlined()) {
4694           Klass* klass = nonstatic_inline_type_klasses[next_inline_type_index];
4695           assert(klass != NULL, "Klass should have been loaded and resolved earlier");
4696           assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(),"Must be an inline type");
4697           ValueKlass* vklass = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4698           real_offset = next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset;
4699           next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset += (vklass->size_helper()) * wordSize - vklass->first_field_offset();
4700           // aligning next inline type on a 64 bits boundary
4701           next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset, BytesPerLong);
4702           next_inline_type_index += 1;
4703 
4704           if (vklass->contains_oops()) { // add flatten oop maps
4705             int diff = real_offset - vklass->first_field_offset();
4706             const OopMapBlock* map = vklass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps();
4707             const OopMapBlock* const last_map = map + vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4708             while (map < last_map) {
4709               nonstatic_oop_maps->add(map->offset() + diff, map->count());
4710               map++;
4711             }
4712           }
4713           break;
4714         } else {
4715           // Fall through
4716         }
4717       case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4718         if( nonstatic_oop_space_count > 0 ) {
4719           real_offset = nonstatic_oop_space_offset;
4720           nonstatic_oop_space_offset += heapOopSize;
4721           nonstatic_oop_space_count  -= 1;
4722         } else {
4723           real_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset;
4724           next_nonstatic_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4725         }
4726         nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4727         break;
4728       case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4729         if( nonstatic_byte_space_count > 0 ) {
4730           real_offset = nonstatic_byte_space_offset;
4731           nonstatic_byte_space_offset += 1;
4732           nonstatic_byte_space_count  -= 1;
4733         } else {
4734           real_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset;
4735           next_nonstatic_byte_offset += 1;
4736         }
4737         break;
4738       case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4739         if( nonstatic_short_space_count > 0 ) {
4740           real_offset = nonstatic_short_space_offset;
4741           nonstatic_short_space_offset += BytesPerShort;
4742           nonstatic_short_space_count  -= 1;
4743         } else {
4744           real_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset;
4745           next_nonstatic_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4746         }
4747         break;
4748       case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4749         if( nonstatic_word_space_count > 0 ) {
4750           real_offset = nonstatic_word_space_offset;
4751           nonstatic_word_space_offset += BytesPerInt;
4752           nonstatic_word_space_count  -= 1;
4753         } else {
4754           real_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset;
4755           next_nonstatic_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4756         }
4757         break;
4758       case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4759         real_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4760         next_nonstatic_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4761         break;
4762       default:
4763         ShouldNotReachHere();
4764     }
4765     fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4766   }
4767 
4768 
4769   // Handle the contended cases.
4770   //
4771   // Each contended field should not intersect the cache line with another contended field.
4772   // In the absence of alignment information, we end up with pessimistically separating
4773   // the fields with full-width padding.
4774   //
4775   // Additionally, this should not break alignment for the fields, so we round the alignment up
4776   // for each field.
4777   if (nonstatic_contended_count > 0) {
4778 
4779     // if there is at least one contended field, we need to have pre-padding for them
4780     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4781 
4782     // collect all contended groups
4783     ResourceBitMap bm(cp->size());
4784     for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4785       // skip already laid out fields
4786       if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4787 
4788       if (fs.is_contended()) {
4789         bm.set_bit(fs.contended_group());
4790       }
4791     }
4792 
4793     int current_group = -1;
4794     while ((current_group = (int)bm.get_next_one_offset(current_group + 1)) != (int)bm.size()) {
4795 
4796       for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4797 
4798         // skip already laid out fields
4799         if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4800 
4801         // skip non-contended fields and fields from different group
4802         if (!fs.is_contended() || (fs.contended_group() != current_group)) continue;
4803 
4804         // handle statics below
4805         if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4806 
4807         int real_offset = 0;
4808         FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4809 
4810         switch (atype) {
4811           case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4812             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, 1);
4813             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4814             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += 1;
4815             break;
4816 
4817           case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4818             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerShort);
4819             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4820             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerShort;
4821             break;
4822 
4823           case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4824             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerInt);
4825             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4826             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerInt;
4827             break;
4828 
4829           case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4830             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4831             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4832             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerLong;
4833             break;
4834 
4835             // Inline types in static fields are handled with oops
4836           case NONSTATIC_INLINE:
4837             throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
4838                                       "@Contended annotation not supported for inline types yet", fs.name(), fs.signature());
4839             return;
4840 
4841           case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4842             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, heapOopSize);
4843             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4844             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += heapOopSize;
4845             nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4846             break;
4847 
4848           default:
4849             ShouldNotReachHere();
4850         }
4851 
4852         if (fs.contended_group() == 0) {
4853           // Contended group defines the equivalence class over the fields:
4854           // the fields within the same contended group are not inter-padded.
4855           // The only exception is default group, which does not incur the
4856           // equivalence, and so requires intra-padding.
4857           next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4858         }
4859 
4860         fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4861       } // for
4862 
4863       // Start laying out the next group.
4864       // Note that this will effectively pad the last group in the back;
4865       // this is expected to alleviate memory contention effects for
4866       // subclass fields and/or adjacent object.
4867       // If this was the default group, the padding is already in place.
4868       if (current_group != 0) {
4869         next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4870       }
4871     }
4872 
4873     // handle static fields
4874   }
4875 
4876   // Entire class is contended, pad in the back.
4877   // This helps to alleviate memory contention effects for subclass fields
4878   // and/or adjacent object.
4879   if (is_contended_class) {
4880     assert(!is_inline_type(), "@Contended not supported for inline types yet");
4881     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4882   }
4883 
4884   int notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end;
4885   if (nonstatic_inline_type_count != 0) {
4886     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset;
4887   } else {
4888     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4889   }
4890 
4891   int nonstatic_field_sz_align = heapOopSize;
4892   if (is_inline_type()) {
4893     if ((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) > heapOopSize) {
4894       nonstatic_field_sz_align = BytesPerLong; // value copy of fields only uses jlong copy
4895     }
4896   }
4897   int nonstatic_fields_end      = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, nonstatic_field_sz_align);
4898   int instance_end              = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, wordSize);
4899   int static_fields_end         = align_up(next_static_byte_offset, wordSize);
4900 
4901   int static_field_size         = (static_fields_end -
4902                                    InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields()) / wordSize;
4903   nonstatic_field_size          = nonstatic_field_size +
4904                                   (nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) / heapOopSize;
4905 
4906   int instance_size             = align_object_size(instance_end / wordSize);
4907 
4908   assert(instance_size == align_object_size(align_up(
4909          (instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() + nonstatic_field_size*heapOopSize)
4910          + initial_inline_type_padding, wordSize) / wordSize), "consistent layout helper value");
4911 
4912 
4913   // Invariant: nonstatic_field end/start should only change if there are
4914   // nonstatic fields in the class, or if the class is contended. We compare
4915   // against the non-aligned value, so that end alignment will not fail the
4916   // assert without actually having the fields.
4917   assert((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end == nonstatic_fields_start) ||
4918          is_contended_class ||
4919          (nonstatic_fields_count > 0), "double-check nonstatic start/end");
4920 
4921   // Number of non-static oop map blocks allocated at end of klass.
4922   nonstatic_oop_maps->compact();
4923 
4924 #ifndef PRODUCT
4925   if ((PrintFieldLayout && !is_inline_type()) ||
4926       (PrintInlineLayout && (is_inline_type() || has_nonstatic_inline_fields))) {
4927     print_field_layout(_class_name,
4928           _fields,
4929           cp,
4930           instance_size,
4931           nonstatic_fields_start,
4932           nonstatic_fields_end,
4933           static_fields_end);
4934     nonstatic_oop_maps->print_on(tty);
4935     tty->print("\n");
4936     tty->print_cr("Instance size = %d", instance_size);
4937     tty->print_cr("Nonstatic_field_size = %d", nonstatic_field_size);
4938     tty->print_cr("Static_field_size = %d", static_field_size);
4939     tty->print_cr("Has nonstatic fields = %d", has_nonstatic_fields);
4940     tty->print_cr("---");
4941   }
4942 
4943 #endif
4944   // Pass back information needed for InstanceKlass creation
4945   info->oop_map_blocks = nonstatic_oop_maps;
4946   info->_instance_size = instance_size;
4947   info->_static_field_size = static_field_size;
4948   info->_nonstatic_field_size = nonstatic_field_size;
4949   info->_has_nonstatic_fields = has_nonstatic_fields;
4950   info->_has_inline_fields = nonstatic_inline_type_count > 0;
4951 
4952   // An inline type is naturally atomic if it has just one field, and
4953   // that field is simple enough.
4954   info->_is_naturally_atomic = (is_inline_type() &&
4955                                 !super_has_nonstatic_fields &&
4956                                 (nonstatic_fields_count <= 1) &&
4957                                 (not_atomic_inline_types == 0) &&
4958                                 (nonstatic_contended_count == 0));
4959   // This may be too restrictive, since if all the fields fit in 64
4960   // bits we could make the decision to align instances of this class
4961   // to 64-bit boundaries, and load and store them as single words.
4962   // And on machines which supported larger atomics we could similarly
4963   // allow larger values to be atomic, if properly aligned.
4964 }
4965 
4966 void ClassFileParser::set_precomputed_flags(InstanceKlass* ik) {
4967   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
4968 
4969   const Klass* const super = ik->super();
4970 
4971   // Check if this klass has an empty finalize method (i.e. one with return bytecode only),
4972   // in which case we don't have to register objects as finalizable
4973   if (!_has_empty_finalizer) {
4974     if (_has_finalizer ||
4975         (super != NULL && super->has_finalizer())) {
4976       ik->set_has_finalizer();
4977     }
4978   }
4979 
4980 #ifdef ASSERT
4981   bool f = false;
4982   const Method* const m = ik->lookup_method(vmSymbols::finalize_method_name(),
4983                                            vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
4984   if (m != NULL && !m->is_empty_method()) {
4985       f = true;
4986   }
4987 
4988   // Spec doesn't prevent agent from redefinition of empty finalizer.
4989   // Despite the fact that it's generally bad idea and redefined finalizer
4990   // will not work as expected we shouldn't abort vm in this case
4991   if (!ik->has_redefined_this_or_super()) {
4992     assert(ik->has_finalizer() == f, "inconsistent has_finalizer");
4993   }
4994 #endif
4995 
4996   // Check if this klass supports the java.lang.Cloneable interface
4997   if (SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass_loaded()) {
4998     if (ik->is_subtype_of(SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass())) {
4999       if (ik->is_inline_klass()) {
5000         Thread *THREAD = Thread::current();
5001         throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support Cloneable");
5002         return;
5003       }
5004       ik->set_is_cloneable();
5005     }
5006   }
5007 
5008   // Check if this klass has a vanilla default constructor
5009   if (super == NULL) {
5010     // java.lang.Object has empty default constructor
5011     ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
5012   } else {
5013     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor() &&
5014         _has_vanilla_constructor) {
5015       ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
5016     }
5017 #ifdef ASSERT
5018     bool v = false;
5019     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor()) {
5020       const Method* const constructor =
5021         ik->find_method(vmSymbols::object_initializer_name(),
5022                        vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
5023       if (constructor != NULL && constructor->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
5024         v = true;
5025       }
5026     }
5027     assert(v == ik->has_vanilla_constructor(), "inconsistent has_vanilla_constructor");
5028 #endif
5029   }
5030 
5031   // If it cannot be fast-path allocated, set a bit in the layout helper.
5032   // See documentation of InstanceKlass::can_be_fastpath_allocated().
5033   assert(ik->size_helper() > 0, "layout_helper is initialized");
5034   if ((!RegisterFinalizersAtInit && ik->has_finalizer())
5035       || ik->is_abstract() || ik->is_interface()
5036       || (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Class() && ik->class_loader() == NULL)
5037       || ik->size_helper() >= FastAllocateSizeLimit) {
5038     // Forbid fast-path allocation.
5039     const jint lh = Klass::instance_layout_helper(ik->size_helper(), true);
5040     ik->set_layout_helper(lh);
5041   }
5042 }
5043 
5044 bool ClassFileParser::supports_inline_types() const {
5045   // Inline types are only supported by class file version 55 and later
5046   return _major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION;
5047 }
5048 
5049 // utility methods for appending an array with check for duplicates
5050 
5051 static void append_interfaces(GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* result,
5052                               const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const ifs) {
5053   // iterate over new interfaces
5054   for (int i = 0; i < ifs->length(); i++) {
5055     InstanceKlass* const e = ifs->at(i);
5056     assert(e->is_klass() && e->is_interface(), "just checking");
5057     // add new interface
5058     result->append_if_missing(e);
5059   }
5060 }
5061 
5062 static Array<InstanceKlass*>* compute_transitive_interfaces(const InstanceKlass* super,
5063                                                             Array<InstanceKlass*>* local_ifs,
5064                                                             ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
5065                                                             TRAPS) {
5066   assert(local_ifs != NULL, "invariant");
5067   assert(loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
5068 
5069   // Compute maximum size for transitive interfaces
5070   int max_transitive_size = 0;
5071   int super_size = 0;
5072   // Add superclass transitive interfaces size
5073   if (super != NULL) {
5074     super_size = super->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5075     max_transitive_size += super_size;
5076   }
5077   // Add local interfaces' super interfaces
5078   const int local_size = local_ifs->length();
5079   for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5080     InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5081     max_transitive_size += l->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5082   }
5083   // Finally add local interfaces
5084   max_transitive_size += local_size;
5085   // Construct array
5086   if (max_transitive_size == 0) {
5087     // no interfaces, use canonicalized array
5088     return Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
5089   } else if (max_transitive_size == super_size) {
5090     // no new local interfaces added, share superklass' transitive interface array
5091     return super->transitive_interfaces();
5092     // The three lines below are commented to work around bug JDK-8245487
5093 //  } else if (max_transitive_size == local_size) {
5094 //    // only local interfaces added, share local interface array
5095 //    return local_ifs;
5096   } else {
5097     ResourceMark rm;
5098     GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* const result = new GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>(max_transitive_size);
5099 
5100     // Copy down from superclass
5101     if (super != NULL) {
5102       append_interfaces(result, super->transitive_interfaces());
5103     }
5104 
5105     // Copy down from local interfaces' superinterfaces
5106     for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5107       InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5108       append_interfaces(result, l->transitive_interfaces());
5109     }
5110     // Finally add local interfaces
5111     append_interfaces(result, local_ifs);
5112 
5113     // length will be less than the max_transitive_size if duplicates were removed
5114     const int length = result->length();
5115     assert(length <= max_transitive_size, "just checking");
5116 
5117     if (length == 1 && result->at(0) == SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass()) {
5118       return Universe::the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array();
5119     }
5120
