5121     Array<InstanceKlass*>* const new_result =
5122       MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(loader_data, length, CHECK_NULL);
5123     for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
5124       InstanceKlass* const e = result->at(i);
5125       assert(e != NULL, "just checking");
5126       new_result->at_put(i, e);
5127     }
5128     return new_result;
5129   }
5130 }
5131 
5132 static void check_super_class_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5133   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5134   const Klass* const super = this_klass->super();
5135 
5136   if (super != NULL) {
5137     const InstanceKlass* super_ik = InstanceKlass::cast(super);
5138 
5139     if (super->is_final()) {
5140       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5141       Exceptions::fthrow(
5142         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5143         vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5144         "class %s cannot inherit from final class %s",
5145         this_klass->external_name(),
5146         super_ik->external_name());
5147       return;
5148     }
5149 
5150     if (super_ik->is_sealed() && !super_ik->has_as_permitted_subclass(this_klass)) {
5151       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5152       Exceptions::fthrow(
5153         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5154         vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
5155         "class %s cannot inherit from sealed class %s",
5156         this_klass->external_name(),
5157         super_ik->external_name());
5158       return;
5159     }
5160 
5161     // If the loader is not the boot loader then throw an exception if its
5162     // superclass is in package jdk.internal.reflect and its loader is not a
5163     // special reflection class loader
5164     if (!this_klass->class_loader_data()->is_the_null_class_loader_data()) {
5165       PackageEntry* super_package = super->package();
5166       if (super_package != NULL &&
5167           super_package->name()->fast_compare(vmSymbols::jdk_internal_reflect()) == 0 &&
5168           !java_lang_ClassLoader::is_reflection_class_loader(this_klass->class_loader())) {
5169         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5170         Exceptions::fthrow(
5171           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5172           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5173           "class %s loaded by %s cannot access jdk/internal/reflect superclass %s",
5174           this_klass->external_name(),
5175           this_klass->class_loader_data()->loader_name_and_id(),
5176           super->external_name());
5177         return;
5178       }
5179     }
5180 
5181     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5182       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, InstanceKlass::cast(super), false);
5183     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5184       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5185       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5186                                                       InstanceKlass::cast(super),
5187                                                       vca_result);
5188       if (msg == NULL) {
5189         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == super->module());
5190         Exceptions::fthrow(
5191           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5192           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5193           "class %s cannot access its %ssuperclass %s (%s%s%s)",
5194           this_klass->external_name(),
5195           super->is_abstract() ? "abstract " : "",
5196           super->external_name(),
5197           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(super) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5198           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5199           (same_module) ? "" : super->class_in_module_of_loader());
5200       } else {
5201         // Add additional message content.
5202         Exceptions::fthrow(
5203           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5204           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5205           "superclass access check failed: %s",
5206           msg);
5207       }
5208     }
5209   }
5210 }
5211 
5212 
5213 static void check_super_interface_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5214   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5215   const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = this_klass->local_interfaces();
5216   const int lng = local_interfaces->length();
5217   for (int i = lng - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
5218     InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
5219     assert (k != NULL && k->is_interface(), "invalid interface");
5220 
5221     if (k->is_sealed() && !k->has_as_permitted_subclass(this_klass)) {
5222       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5223       Exceptions::fthrow(
5224         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5225         vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
5226         "class %s cannot %s sealed interface %s",
5227         this_klass->external_name(),
5228         this_klass->is_interface() ? "extend" : "implement",
5229         k->external_name());
5230       return;
5231     }
5232 
5233     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5234       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, k, false);
5235     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5236       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5237       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5238                                                       k,
5239                                                       vca_result);
5240       if (msg == NULL) {
5241         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == k->module());
5242         Exceptions::fthrow(
5243           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5244           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5245           "class %s cannot access its superinterface %s (%s%s%s)",
5246           this_klass->external_name(),
5247           k->external_name(),
5248           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(k) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5249           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5250           (same_module) ? "" : k->class_in_module_of_loader());
5251       } else {
5252         // Add additional message content.
5253         Exceptions::fthrow(
5254           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5255           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5256           "superinterface check failed: %s",
5257           msg);
5258       }
5259     }
5260   }
5261 }
5262 
5263 
5264 static void check_final_method_override(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5265   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5266   const Array<Method*>* const methods = this_klass->methods();
5267   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5268 
5269   // go thru each method and check if it overrides a final method
5270   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5271     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5272 
5273     // skip private, static, and <init> methods
5274     if ((!m->is_private() && !m->is_static()) &&
5275         (m->name() != vmSymbols::object_initializer_name())) {
5276 
5277       const Symbol* const name = m->name();
5278       const Symbol* const signature = m->signature();
5279       const Klass* k = this_klass->super();
5280       const Method* super_m = NULL;
5281       while (k != NULL) {
5282         // skip supers that don't have final methods.
5283         if (k->has_final_method()) {
5284           // lookup a matching method in the super class hierarchy
5285           super_m = InstanceKlass::cast(k)->lookup_method(name, signature);
5286           if (super_m == NULL) {
5287             break; // didn't find any match; get out
5288           }
5289 
5290           if (super_m->is_final() && !super_m->is_static() &&
5291               !super_m->access_flags().is_private()) {
5292             // matching method in super is final, and not static or private
5293             bool can_access = Reflection::verify_member_access(this_klass,
5294                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5295                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5296                                                                super_m->access_flags(),
5297                                                               false, false, CHECK);
5298             if (can_access) {
5299               // this class can access super final method and therefore override
5300               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5301               Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5302                                  vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5303                                  "class %s overrides final method %s.%s%s",
5304                                  this_klass->external_name(),
5305                                  super_m->method_holder()->external_name(),
5306                                  name->as_C_string(),
5307                                  signature->as_C_string()
5308                                  );
5309               return;
5310             }
5311           }
5312 
5313           // continue to look from super_m's holder's super.
5314           k = super_m->method_holder()->super();
5315           continue;
5316         }
5317 
5318         k = k->super();
5319       }
5320     }
5321   }
5322 }
5323 
5324 
5325 // assumes that this_klass is an interface
5326 static void check_illegal_static_method(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5327   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5328   assert(this_klass->is_interface(), "not an interface");
5329   const Array<Method*>* methods = this_klass->methods();
5330   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5331 
5332   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5333     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5334     // if m is static and not the init method, throw a verify error
5335     if ((m->is_static()) && (m->name() != vmSymbols::class_initializer_name())) {
5336       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5337       Exceptions::fthrow(
5338         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5339         vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5340         "Illegal static method %s in interface %s",
5341         m->name()->as_C_string(),
5342         this_klass->external_name()
5343       );
5344       return;
5345     }
5346   }
5347 }
5348 
5349 // utility methods for format checking
5350 
5351 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_modifiers(jint flags, TRAPS) const {
5352   const bool is_module = (flags & JVM_ACC_MODULE) != 0;
5353   const bool is_inline_type = (flags & JVM_ACC_VALUE) != 0;
5354   assert(_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION || !is_module, "JVM_ACC_MODULE should not be set");
5355   assert(supports_inline_types() || !is_inline_type, "JVM_ACC_VALUE should not be set");
5356   if (is_module) {
5357     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5358     Exceptions::fthrow(
5359       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5360       vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
5361       "%s is not a class because access_flag ACC_MODULE is set",
5362       _class_name->as_C_string());
5363     return;
5364   }
5365 
5366   if (is_inline_type && !EnableValhalla) {
5367     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5368     Exceptions::fthrow(
5369       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5370       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5371       "Class modifier ACC_VALUE in class %s requires option -XX:+EnableValhalla",
5372       _class_name->as_C_string()
5373     );
5374   }
5375 
5376   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5377 
5378   const bool is_interface  = (flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE)  != 0;
5379   const bool is_abstract   = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)   != 0;
5380   const bool is_final      = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)      != 0;
5381   const bool is_super      = (flags & JVM_ACC_SUPER)      != 0;
5382   const bool is_enum       = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)       != 0;
5383   const bool is_annotation = (flags & JVM_ACC_ANNOTATION) != 0;
5384   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5385   const bool major_gte_14  = _major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION;
5386 
5387   if ((is_abstract && is_final) ||
5388       (is_interface && !is_abstract) ||
5389       (is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && (is_super || is_enum)) ||
5390       (!is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && is_annotation) ||
5391       (is_inline_type && (is_interface || is_abstract || is_enum || !is_final))) {
5392     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5393     const char* class_note = "";
5394     if (is_inline_type)  class_note = " (an inline class)";
5395     Exceptions::fthrow(
5396       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5397       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5398       "Illegal class modifiers in class %s%s: 0x%X",
5399       _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags
5400     );
5401     return;
5402   }
5403 }
5404 
5405 static bool has_illegal_visibility(jint flags) {
5406   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5407   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5408   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5409 
5410   return ((is_public && is_protected) ||
5411           (is_public && is_private) ||
5412           (is_protected && is_private));
5413 }
5414 
5415 // A legal major_version.minor_version must be one of the following:
5416 //
5417 //  Major_version >= 45 and major_version < 56, any minor_version.
5418 //  Major_version >= 56 and major_version <= JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 0.
5419 //  Major_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 65535 and --enable-preview is present.
5420 //
5421 static void verify_class_version(u2 major, u2 minor, Symbol* class_name, TRAPS){
5422   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5423   const u2 max_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION;
5424   if (major < JAVA_MIN_SUPPORTED_VERSION) {
5425     Exceptions::fthrow(
5426       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5427       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5428       "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid major version",
5429       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5430     return;
5431   }
5432 
5433   if (major > max_version) {
5434     Exceptions::fthrow(
5435       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5436       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5437       "%s has been compiled by a more recent version of the Java Runtime (class file version %u.%u), "
5438       "this version of the Java Runtime only recognizes class file versions up to %u.0",
5439       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
5440     return;
5441   }
5442 
5443   if (major < JAVA_12_VERSION || minor == 0) {
5444     return;
5445   }
5446 
5447   if (minor == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION) {
5448     if (major != max_version) {
5449       Exceptions::fthrow(
5450         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5451         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5452         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with preview features that are unsupported. "
5453         "This version of the Java Runtime only recognizes preview features for class file version %u.%u",
5454         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION, JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION);
5455       return;
5456     }
5457 
5458     if (!Arguments::enable_preview()) {
5459       Exceptions::fthrow(
5460         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5461         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5462         "Preview features are not enabled for %s (class file version %u.%u). Try running with '--enable-preview'",
5463         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5464       return;
5465     }
5466 
5467   } else { // minor != JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION
5468     Exceptions::fthrow(
5469         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5470         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5471         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid non-zero minor version",
5472         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5473   }
5474 }
5475 
5476 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_modifiers(jint flags,
5477                                                    bool is_interface,
5478                                                    bool is_inline_type,
5479                                                    TRAPS) const {
5480   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5481 
5482   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5483   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5484   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5485   const bool is_static    = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)    != 0;
5486   const bool is_final     = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)     != 0;
5487   const bool is_volatile  = (flags & JVM_ACC_VOLATILE)  != 0;
5488   const bool is_transient = (flags & JVM_ACC_TRANSIENT) != 0;
5489   const bool is_enum      = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)      != 0;
5490   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5491 
5492   bool is_illegal = false;
5493 
5494   if (is_interface) {
5495     if (!is_public || !is_static || !is_final || is_private ||
5496         is_protected || is_volatile || is_transient ||
5497         (major_gte_1_5 && is_enum)) {
5498       is_illegal = true;
5499     }
5500   } else { // not interface
5501     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags) || (is_final && is_volatile)) {
5502       is_illegal = true;
5503     } else {
5504       if (is_inline_type && !is_static && !is_final) {
5505         is_illegal = true;
5506       }
5507     }
5508   }
5509 
5510   if (is_illegal) {
5511     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5512     Exceptions::fthrow(
5513       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5514       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5515       "Illegal field modifiers in class %s: 0x%X",
5516       _class_name->as_C_string(), flags);
5517     return;
5518   }
5519 }
5520 
5521 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_modifiers(jint flags,
5522                                                     bool is_interface,
5523                                                     bool is_inline_type,
5524                                                     const Symbol* name,
5525                                                     TRAPS) const {
5526   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5527 
5528   const bool is_public       = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)       != 0;
5529   const bool is_private      = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)      != 0;
5530   const bool is_static       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)       != 0;
5531   const bool is_final        = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)        != 0;
5532   const bool is_native       = (flags & JVM_ACC_NATIVE)       != 0;
5533   const bool is_abstract     = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)     != 0;
5534   const bool is_bridge       = (flags & JVM_ACC_BRIDGE)       != 0;
5535   const bool is_strict       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STRICT)       != 0;
5536   const bool is_synchronized = (flags & JVM_ACC_SYNCHRONIZED) != 0;
5537   const bool is_protected    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED)    != 0;
5538   const bool major_gte_1_5   = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5539   const bool major_gte_8     = _major_version >= JAVA_8_VERSION;
5540   const bool is_initializer  = (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name());
5541 
5542   bool is_illegal = false;
5543 
5544   const char* class_note = "";
5545 
5546   if (is_interface) {
5547     if (major_gte_8) {
5548       // Class file version is JAVA_8_VERSION or later Methods of
5549       // interfaces may set any of the flags except ACC_PROTECTED,
5550       // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, and ACC_SYNCHRONIZED; they must
5551       // have exactly one of the ACC_PUBLIC or ACC_PRIVATE flags set.
5552       if ((is_public == is_private) || /* Only one of private and public should be true - XNOR */
5553           (is_native || is_protected || is_final || is_synchronized) ||
5554           // If a specific method of a class or interface has its
5555           // ACC_ABSTRACT flag set, it must not have any of its
5556           // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, ACC_PRIVATE, ACC_STATIC,
5557           // ACC_STRICT, or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED flags set.  No need to
5558           // check for ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED as
5559           // those flags are illegal irrespective of ACC_ABSTRACT being set or not.
5560           (is_abstract && (is_private || is_static || is_strict))) {
5561         is_illegal = true;
5562       }
5563     } else if (major_gte_1_5) {
5564       // Class file version in the interval [JAVA_1_5_VERSION, JAVA_8_VERSION)
5565       if (!is_public || is_private || is_protected || is_static || is_final ||
5566           is_synchronized || is_native || !is_abstract || is_strict) {
5567         is_illegal = true;
5568       }
5569     } else {
5570       // Class file version is pre-JAVA_1_5_VERSION
5571       if (!is_public || is_static || is_final || is_native || !is_abstract) {
5572         is_illegal = true;
5573       }
5574     }
5575   } else { // not interface
5576     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags)) {
5577       is_illegal = true;
5578     } else {
5579       if (is_initializer) {
5580         if (is_final || is_synchronized || is_native ||
5581             is_abstract || (major_gte_1_5 && is_bridge)) {
5582           is_illegal = true;
5583         }
5584         if (!is_static && !is_inline_type) {
5585           // OK, an object constructor in a regular class
5586         } else if (is_static && is_inline_type) {
5587           // OK, a static init factory in an inline class
5588         } else {
5589           // but no other combinations are allowed
5590           is_illegal = true;
5591           class_note = (is_inline_type ? " (an inline class)" : " (not an inline class)");
5592         }
5593       } else { // not initializer
5594         if (is_inline_type && is_synchronized && !is_static) {
5595           is_illegal = true;
5596           class_note = " (an inline class)";
5597         } else {
5598           if (is_abstract) {
5599             if ((is_final || is_native || is_private || is_static ||
5600                 (major_gte_1_5 && (is_synchronized || is_strict)))) {
5601               is_illegal = true;
5602             }
5603           }
5604         }
5605       }
5606     }
5607   }
5608 
5609   if (is_illegal) {
5610     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5611     Exceptions::fthrow(
5612       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5613       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5614       "Method %s in class %s%s has illegal modifiers: 0x%X",
5615       name->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags);
5616     return;
5617   }
5618 }
5619 
5620 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_utf8(const unsigned char* buffer,
5621                                         int length,
5622                                         TRAPS) const {
5623   assert(_need_verify, "only called when _need_verify is true");
5624   if (!UTF8::is_legal_utf8(buffer, length, _major_version <= 47)) {
5625     classfile_parse_error("Illegal UTF8 string in constant pool in class file %s", CHECK);
5626   }
5627 }
5628 
5629 // Unqualified names may not contain the characters '.', ';', '[', or '/'.
5630 // In class names, '/' separates unqualified names.  This is verified in this function also.
5631 // Method names also may not contain the characters '<' or '>', unless <init>
5632 // or <clinit>.  Note that method names may not be <init> or <clinit> in this
5633 // method.  Because these names have been checked as special cases before
5634 // calling this method in verify_legal_method_name.
5635 //
5636 // This method is also called from the modular system APIs in modules.cpp
5637 // to verify the validity of module and package names.
5638 bool ClassFileParser::verify_unqualified_name(const char* name,
5639                                               unsigned int length,
5640                                               int type) {
5641   if (length == 0) return false;  // Must have at least one char.
5642   for (const char* p = name; p != name + length; p++) {
5643     switch(*p) {
5644       case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT:
5645       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS:
5646       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5647         // do not permit '.', ';', or '['
5648         return false;
5649       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH:
5650         // check for '//' or leading or trailing '/' which are not legal
5651         // unqualified name must not be empty
5652         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalClass) {
5653           if (p == name || p+1 >= name+length ||
5654               *(p+1) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5655             return false;
5656           }
5657         } else {
5658           return false;   // do not permit '/' unless it's class name
5659         }
5660         break;
5661       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL:
5662       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDSPECIAL:
5663         // do not permit '<' or '>' in method names
5664         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalMethod) {
5665           return false;
5666         }
5667     }
5668   }
5669   return true;
5670 }
5671 
5672 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5673 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5674 // be taken as a fieldname. Allow '/' if slash_ok is true.
5675 // Return a pointer to just past the fieldname.
5676 // Return NULL if no fieldname at all was found, or in the case of slash_ok
5677 // being true, we saw consecutive slashes (meaning we were looking for a
5678 // qualified path but found something that was badly-formed).
5679 static const char* skip_over_field_name(const char* const name,
5680                                         bool slash_ok,
5681                                         unsigned int length) {
5682   const char* p;
5683   jboolean last_is_slash = false;
5684   jboolean not_first_ch = false;
5685 
5686   for (p = name; p != name + length; not_first_ch = true) {
5687     const char* old_p = p;
5688     jchar ch = *p;
5689     if (ch < 128) {
5690       p++;
5691       // quick check for ascii
5692       if ((ch >= 'a' && ch <= 'z') ||
5693         (ch >= 'A' && ch <= 'Z') ||
5694         (ch == '_' || ch == '$') ||
5695         (not_first_ch && ch >= '0' && ch <= '9')) {
5696         last_is_slash = false;
5697         continue;
5698       }
5699       if (slash_ok && ch == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5700         if (last_is_slash) {
5701           return NULL;  // Don't permit consecutive slashes
5702         }
5703         last_is_slash = true;
5704         continue;
5705       }
5706     }
5707     else {
5708       jint unicode_ch;
5709       char* tmp_p = UTF8::next_character(p, &unicode_ch);
5710       p = tmp_p;
5711       last_is_slash = false;
5712       // Check if ch is Java identifier start or is Java identifier part
5713       // 4672820: call java.lang.Character methods directly without generating separate tables.
5714       EXCEPTION_MARK;
5715       // return value
5716       JavaValue result(T_BOOLEAN);
5717       // Set up the arguments to isJavaIdentifierStart or isJavaIdentifierPart
5718       JavaCallArguments args;
5719       args.push_int(unicode_ch);
5720 
5721       if (not_first_ch) {
5722         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierPart(char ch);
5723         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5724           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5725           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierPart_name(),
5726           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5727           &args,
5728           THREAD);
5729       } else {
5730         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierStart(char ch);
5731         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5732           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5733           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierStart_name(),
5734           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5735           &args,
5736           THREAD);
5737       }
5738       if (HAS_PENDING_EXCEPTION) {
5739         CLEAR_PENDING_EXCEPTION;
5740         return NULL;
5741       }
5742       if(result.get_jboolean()) {
5743         continue;
5744       }
5745     }
5746     return (not_first_ch) ? old_p : NULL;
5747   }
5748   return (not_first_ch) ? p : NULL;
5749 }
5750 
5751 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5752 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5753 // be taken as a field signature. Allow "void" if void_ok.
5754 // Return a pointer to just past the signature.
5755 // Return NULL if no legal signature is found.
5756 const char* ClassFileParser::skip_over_field_signature(const char* signature,
5757                                                        bool void_ok,
5758                                                        unsigned int length,
5759                                                        TRAPS) const {
5760   unsigned int array_dim = 0;
5761   while (length > 0) {
5762     switch (signature[0]) {
5763     case JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID: if (!void_ok) { return NULL; }
5764     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BOOLEAN:
5765     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BYTE:
5766     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CHAR:
5767     case JVM_SIGNATURE_SHORT:
5768     case JVM_SIGNATURE_INT:
5769     case JVM_SIGNATURE_FLOAT:
5770     case JVM_SIGNATURE_LONG:
5771     case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOUBLE:
5772       return signature + 1;
5773     case JVM_SIGNATURE_INLINE_TYPE:
5774       // Can't enable this check until JDK upgrades the bytecode generators
5775       // if (_major_version < CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS ) {
5776       //   classfile_parse_error("Class name contains illegal Q-signature "
5777       //                                    "in descriptor in class file %s",
5778       //                                    CHECK_0);
5779       // }
5780       // fall through
5781     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CLASS:
5782     {
5783       if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5784         // Skip over the class name if one is there
5785         const char* const p = skip_over_field_name(signature + 1, true, --length);
5786 
5787         // The next character better be a semicolon
5788         if (p && (p - signature) > 1 && p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS) {
5789           return p + 1;
5790         }
5791       }
5792       else {
5793         // Skip leading 'L' or 'Q' and ignore first appearance of ';'
5794         signature++;
5795         const char* c = (const char*) memchr(signature, JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS, length - 1);
5796         // Format check signature
5797         if (c != NULL) {
5798           int newlen = c - (char*) signature;
5799           bool legal = verify_unqualified_name(signature, newlen, LegalClass);
5800           if (!legal) {
5801             classfile_parse_error("Class name is empty or contains illegal character "
5802                                   "in descriptor in class file %s",
5803                                   CHECK_NULL);
5804             return NULL;
5805           }
5806           return signature + newlen + 1;
5807         }
5808       }
5809       return NULL;
5810     }
5811     case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5812       array_dim++;
5813       if (array_dim > 255) {
5814         // 4277370: array descriptor is valid only if it represents 255 or fewer dimensions.
5815         classfile_parse_error("Array type descriptor has more than 255 dimensions in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
5816       }
5817       // The rest of what's there better be a legal signature
5818       signature++;
5819       length--;
5820       void_ok = false;
5821       break;
5822     default:
5823       return NULL;
5824     }
5825   }
5826   return NULL;
5827 }
5828 
5829 // Checks if name is a legal class name.
5830 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5831   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5832 
5833   assert(name->refcount() > 0, "symbol must be kept alive");
5834   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5835   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5836   bool legal = false;
5837 
5838   if (length > 0) {
5839     const char* p;
5840     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY) {
5841       p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5842       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5843     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5844       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5845         p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, true, length);
5846         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5847       }
5848     } else if (_major_version >= CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS && bytes[length - 1] == ';' ) {
5849       // Support for L...; and Q...; descriptors
5850       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes + 1, length - 2, LegalClass);
5851     } else {
5852       // 4900761: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5853       // Class names may be drawn from the entire Unicode character set.
5854       // Identifiers between '/' must be unqualified names.
5855       // The utf8 string has been verified when parsing cpool entries.
5856       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalClass);
5857     }
5858   }
5859   if (!legal) {
5860     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5861     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5862     Exceptions::fthrow(
5863       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5864       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5865       "Illegal class name \"%.*s\" in class file %s", length, bytes,
5866       _class_name->as_C_string()
5867     );
5868     return;
5869   }
5870 }
5871 
5872 // Checks if name is a legal field name.
5873 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5874   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5875 
5876   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5877   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5878   bool legal = false;
5879 
5880   if (length > 0) {
5881     if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5882       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5883         const char* p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5884         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5885       }
5886     } else {
5887       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5888       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalField);
5889     }
5890   }
5891 
5892   if (!legal) {
5893     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5894     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5895     Exceptions::fthrow(
5896       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5897       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5898       "Illegal field name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5899       _class_name->as_C_string()
5900     );
5901     return;
5902   }
5903 }
5904 
5905 // Checks if name is a legal method name.
5906 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5907   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5908 
5909   assert(name != NULL, "method name is null");
5910   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5911   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5912   bool legal = false;
5913 
5914   if (length > 0) {
5915     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5916       if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name() || name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name()) {
5917         legal = true;
5918       }
5919     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5920       const char* p;
5921       p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5922       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5923     } else {
5924       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5925       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalMethod);
5926     }
5927   }
5928 
5929   if (!legal) {
5930     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5931     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5932     Exceptions::fthrow(
5933       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5934       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5935       "Illegal method name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5936       _class_name->as_C_string()
5937     );
5938     return;
5939   }
5940 }
5941 
5942 
5943 // Checks if signature is a legal field signature.
5944 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_signature(const Symbol* name,
5945                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5946                                                    TRAPS) const {
5947   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5948 
5949   const char* const bytes = (const char* const)signature->bytes();
5950   const unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5951   const char* const p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5952 
5953   if (p == NULL || (p - bytes) != (int)length) {
5954     throwIllegalSignature("Field", name, signature, CHECK);
5955   }
5956 }
5957 
5958 // Checks if signature is a legal method signature.
5959 // Returns number of parameters
5960 int ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_signature(const Symbol* name,
5961                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5962                                                    TRAPS) const {
5963   if (!_need_verify) {
5964     // make sure caller's args_size will be less than 0 even for non-static
5965     // method so it will be recomputed in compute_size_of_parameters().
5966     return -2;
5967   }
5968 
5969   // Class initializers cannot have args for class format version >= 51.
5970   if (name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name() &&
5971       signature != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() &&
5972       _major_version >= JAVA_7_VERSION) {
5973     throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
5974     return 0;
5975   }
5976 
5977   unsigned int args_size = 0;
5978   const char* p = (const char*)signature->bytes();
5979   unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5980   const char* nextp;
5981 
5982   // The first character must be a '('
5983   if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_FUNC)) {
5984     length--;
5985     // Skip over legal field signatures
5986     nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5987     while ((length > 0) && (nextp != NULL)) {
5988       args_size++;
5989       if (p[0] == 'J' || p[0] == 'D') {
5990         args_size++;
5991       }
5992       length -= nextp - p;
5993       p = nextp;
5994       nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5995     }
5996     // The first non-signature thing better be a ')'
5997     if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDFUNC)) {
5998       length--;
5999       if (name->utf8_length() > 0 && name->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
6000         // All constructor methods must return void
6001         if ((length == 1) && (p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID)) {
6002           return args_size;
6003         }
6004         // All static init methods must return the current class
6005         if ((length >= 3) && (p[length-1] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS)
6006             && name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
6007           nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
6008           if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
6009             // The actual class will be checked against current class
6010             // when the method is defined (see parse_method).
6011             // A reference to a static init with a bad return type
6012             // will load and verify OK, but will fail to link.
6013             return args_size;
6014           }
6015         }
6016         // The distinction between static factory methods and
6017         // constructors depends on the JVM_ACC_STATIC modifier.
6018         // This distinction must be reflected in a void or non-void
6019         // return. For declared methods, the check is in parse_method.
6020       } else {
6021         // Now we better just have a return value
6022         nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
6023         if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
6024           return args_size;
6025         }
6026       }
6027     }
6028   }
6029   // Report error
6030   throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
6031   return 0;
6032 }
6033 
6034 int ClassFileParser::static_field_size() const {
6035   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6036   return _field_info->_static_field_size;
6037 }
6038 
6039 int ClassFileParser::total_oop_map_count() const {
6040   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6041   return _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count;
6042 }
6043 
6044 jint ClassFileParser::layout_size() const {
6045   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6046   return _field_info->_instance_size;
6047 }
6048 
6049 static void check_methods_for_intrinsics(const InstanceKlass* ik,
6050                                          const Array<Method*>* methods) {
6051   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
6052   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
6053 
6054   // Set up Method*::intrinsic_id as soon as we know the names of methods.
6055   // (We used to do this lazily, but now we query it in Rewriter,
6056   // which is eagerly done for every method, so we might as well do it now,
6057   // when everything is fresh in memory.)
6058   const vmSymbols::SID klass_id = Method::klass_id_for_intrinsics(ik);
6059 
6060   if (klass_id != vmSymbols::NO_SID) {
6061     for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
6062       Method* method = methods->at(j);
6063       method->init_intrinsic_id();
6064 
6065       if (CheckIntrinsics) {
6066         // Check if an intrinsic is defined for method 'method',
6067         // but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.
6068         if (method->intrinsic_id() != vmIntrinsics::_none &&
6069             !method->intrinsic_candidate()) {
6070               tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
6071               "but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.%s",
6072               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
6073               NOT_DEBUG(" Method will not be inlined.") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6074             );
6075           tty->cr();
6076           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6077         }
6078         // Check is the method 'method' is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate,
6079         // but there is no intrinsic available for it.
6080         if (method->intrinsic_candidate() &&
6081           method->intrinsic_id() == vmIntrinsics::_none) {
6082             tty->print("Method [%s] is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate, "
6083               "but no compiler intrinsic is defined for the method.%s",
6084               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
6085               NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6086             );
6087           tty->cr();
6088           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6089         }
6090       }
6091     } // end for
6092 
6093 #ifdef ASSERT
6094     if (CheckIntrinsics) {
6095       // Check for orphan methods in the current class. A method m
6096       // of a class C is orphan if an intrinsic is defined for method m,
6097       // but class C does not declare m.
6098       // The check is potentially expensive, therefore it is available
6099       // only in debug builds.
6100 
6101       for (int id = vmIntrinsics::FIRST_ID; id < (int)vmIntrinsics::ID_LIMIT; ++id) {
6102         if (vmIntrinsics::_compiledLambdaForm == id) {
6103           // The _compiledLamdbdaForm intrinsic is a special marker for bytecode
6104           // generated for the JVM from a LambdaForm and therefore no method
6105           // is defined for it.
6106           continue;
6107         }
6108 
6109         if (vmIntrinsics::class_for(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id)) == klass_id) {
6110           // Check if the current class contains a method with the same
6111           // name, flags, signature.
6112           bool match = false;
6113           for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
6114             const Method* method = methods->at(j);
6115             if (method->intrinsic_id() == id) {
6116               match = true;
6117               break;
6118             }
6119           }
6120 
6121           if (!match) {
6122             char buf[1000];
6123             tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
6124                        "but the method is not available in class [%s].%s",
6125                         vmIntrinsics::short_name_as_C_string(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id),
6126                                                              buf, sizeof(buf)),
6127                         ik->name()->as_C_string(),
6128                         NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6129             );
6130             tty->cr();
6131             DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6132           }
6133         }
6134       } // end for
6135     } // CheckIntrinsics
6136 #endif // ASSERT
6137   }
6138 }
6139 
6140 InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::create_instance_klass(bool changed_by_loadhook,
6141                                                       const ClassInstanceInfo& cl_inst_info,
6142                                                       TRAPS) {
6143   if (_klass != NULL) {
6144     return _klass;
6145   }
6146 
6147   InstanceKlass* const ik =
6148     InstanceKlass::allocate_instance_klass(*this, CHECK_NULL);
6149 
6150   if (is_hidden()) {
6151     mangle_hidden_class_name(ik);
6152   }
6153 
6154   fill_instance_klass(ik, changed_by_loadhook, cl_inst_info, CHECK_NULL);
6155 
6156   assert(_klass == ik, "invariant");
6157 
6158 
6159   if (ik->should_store_fingerprint()) {
6160     ik->store_fingerprint(_stream->compute_fingerprint());
6161   }
6162 
6163   ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(false);
6164   if (UseAOT && ik->supers_have_passed_fingerprint_checks()) {
6165     uint64_t aot_fp = AOTLoader::get_saved_fingerprint(ik);
6166     uint64_t fp = ik->has_stored_fingerprint() ? ik->get_stored_fingerprint() : _stream->compute_fingerprint();
6167     if (aot_fp != 0 && aot_fp == fp) {
6168       // This class matches with a class saved in an AOT library
6169       ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(true);
6170     } else {
6171       ResourceMark rm;
6172       log_info(class, fingerprint)("%s :  expected = " PTR64_FORMAT " actual = " PTR64_FORMAT,
6173                                  ik->external_name(), aot_fp, _stream->compute_fingerprint());
6174     }
6175   }
6176 
6177   if (ik->is_inline_klass()) {
6178     ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(ik);
6179     oop val = ik->allocate_instance(CHECK_NULL);
6180     vk->set_default_value(val);
6181   }
6182 
6183   return ik;
6184 }
6185 
6186 // Return true if the specified class is not a valid super class for an inline type.
6187 // A valid super class for an inline type is abstract, has no instance fields,
6188 // does not implement interface java.lang.IdentityObject (checked elsewhere), has
6189 // an empty body-less no-arg constructor, and no synchronized instance methods.
6190 // This function doesn't check if the class's super types are invalid.  Those checks
6191 // are done elsewhere.  The final determination of whether or not a class is an
6192 // invalid super type for an inline class is done in fill_instance_klass().
6193 bool ClassFileParser::is_invalid_super_for_inline_type() {
6194   if (class_name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6195     return true;
6196   }
6197   if (is_interface() || class_name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
6198     return false;
6199   }
6200   if (!access_flags().is_abstract() || _has_nonstatic_fields) {
6201     return true;
6202   } else {
6203     // Look at each method
6204     for (int x = 0; x < _methods->length(); x++) {
6205       const Method* const method = _methods->at(x);
6206       if (method->is_synchronized() && !method->is_static()) {
6207         return true;
6208 
6209       } else if (method->name() == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
6210         if (method->signature() != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() ||
6211             !method->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
6212           return true;
6213         }
6214       }
6215     }
6216   }
6217   return false;
6218 }
6219 
6220 void ClassFileParser::fill_instance_klass(InstanceKlass* ik,
6221                                           bool changed_by_loadhook,
6222                                           const ClassInstanceInfo& cl_inst_info,
6223                                           TRAPS) {
6224   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
6225 
6226   // Set name and CLD before adding to CLD
6227   ik->set_class_loader_data(_loader_data);
6228   ik->set_name(_class_name);
6229 
6230   // Add all classes to our internal class loader list here,
6231   // including classes in the bootstrap (NULL) class loader.
6232   const bool publicize = !is_internal();
6233 
6234   _loader_data->add_class(ik, publicize);
6235 
6236   set_klass_to_deallocate(ik);
6237 
6238   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6239   assert(ik->static_field_size() == _field_info->_static_field_size, "sanity");
6240   assert(ik->nonstatic_oop_map_count() == _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count,
6241          "sanity");
6242 
6243   assert(ik->is_instance_klass(), "sanity");
6244   assert(ik->size_helper() == _field_info->_instance_size, "sanity");
6245 
6246   // Fill in information already parsed
6247   ik->set_should_verify_class(_need_verify);
6248 
6249   // Not yet: supers are done below to support the new subtype-checking fields
6250   ik->set_nonstatic_field_size(_field_info->_nonstatic_field_size);
6251   ik->set_has_nonstatic_fields(_field_info->_has_nonstatic_fields);
6252   if (_field_info->_is_naturally_atomic && ik->is_inline_klass()) {
6253     ik->set_is_naturally_atomic();
6254   }
6255   if (_is_empty_inline_type) {
6256     ik->set_is_empty_inline_type();
6257   }
6258 
6259   if (this->_invalid_inline_super) {
6260     ik->set_invalid_inline_super();
6261   }
6262 
6263   if (_has_injected_identityObject) {
6264     ik->set_has_injected_identityObject();
6265   }
6266 
6267   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
6268   ik->set_static_oop_field_count(_fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + _fac->count[STATIC_INLINE]);
6269 
6270   // this transfers ownership of a lot of arrays from
6271   // the parser onto the InstanceKlass*
6272   apply_parsed_class_metadata(ik, _java_fields_count, CHECK);
6273 
6274   // can only set dynamic nest-host after static nest information is set
6275   if (cl_inst_info.dynamic_nest_host() != NULL) {
6276     ik->set_nest_host(cl_inst_info.dynamic_nest_host(), THREAD);
6277   }
6278 
6279   // note that is not safe to use the fields in the parser from this point on
6280   assert(NULL == _cp, "invariant");
6281   assert(NULL == _fields, "invariant");
6282   assert(NULL == _methods, "invariant");
6283   assert(NULL == _inner_classes, "invariant");
6284   assert(NULL == _nest_members, "invariant");
6285   assert(NULL == _combined_annotations, "invariant");
6286   assert(NULL == _record_components, "invariant");
6287   assert(NULL == _permitted_subclasses, "invariant");
6288 
6289   if (_has_final_method) {
6290     ik->set_has_final_method();
6291   }
6292 
6293   ik->copy_method_ordering(_method_ordering, CHECK);
6294   // The InstanceKlass::_methods_jmethod_ids cache
6295   // is managed on the assumption that the initial cache
6296   // size is equal to the number of methods in the class. If
6297   // that changes, then InstanceKlass::idnum_can_increment()
6298   // has to be changed accordingly.
6299   ik->set_initial_method_idnum(ik->methods()->length());
6300 
6301   ik->set_this_class_index(_this_class_index);
6302 
6303   if (_is_hidden || is_unsafe_anonymous()) {
6304     // _this_class_index is a CONSTANT_Class entry that refers to this
6305     // hidden or anonymous class itself. If this class needs to refer to its own
6306     // methods or fields, it would use a CONSTANT_MethodRef, etc, which would reference
6307     // _this_class_index. However, because this class is hidden or anonymous (it's
6308     // not stored in SystemDictionary), _this_class_index cannot be resolved
6309     // with ConstantPool::klass_at_impl, which does a SystemDictionary lookup.
6310     // Therefore, we must eagerly resolve _this_class_index now.
6311     ik->constants()->klass_at_put(_this_class_index, ik);
6312   }
6313 
6314   ik->set_minor_version(_minor_version);
6315   ik->set_major_version(_major_version);
6316   ik->set_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6317   ik->set_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6318   if (_is_declared_atomic) {
6319     ik->set_is_declared_atomic();
6320   }
6321 
6322   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6323     assert (ik->is_unsafe_anonymous(), "should be the same");
6324     ik->set_unsafe_anonymous_host(_unsafe_anonymous_host);
6325   }
6326   if (_is_hidden) {
6327     ik->set_is_hidden();
6328   }
6329 
6330   // Set PackageEntry for this_klass
6331   oop cl = ik->class_loader();
6332   Handle clh = Handle(THREAD, java_lang_ClassLoader::non_reflection_class_loader(cl));
6333   ClassLoaderData* cld = ClassLoaderData::class_loader_data_or_null(clh());
6334   ik->set_package(cld, NULL, CHECK);
6335 
6336   const Array<Method*>* const methods = ik->methods();
6337   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
6338   const int methods_len = methods->length();
6339 
6340   check_methods_for_intrinsics(ik, methods);
6341 
6342   // Fill in field values obtained by parse_classfile_attributes
6343   if (_parsed_annotations->has_any_annotations()) {
6344     _parsed_annotations->apply_to(ik);
6345   }
6346 
6347   apply_parsed_class_attributes(ik);
6348 
6349   // Miranda methods
6350   if ((_num_miranda_methods > 0) ||
6351       // if this class introduced new miranda methods or
6352       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_miranda_methods())
6353         // super class exists and this class inherited miranda methods
6354      ) {
6355        ik->set_has_miranda_methods(); // then set a flag
6356   }
6357 
6358   // Fill in information needed to compute superclasses.
6359   ik->initialize_supers(const_cast<InstanceKlass*>(_super_klass), _transitive_interfaces, CHECK);
6360   ik->set_transitive_interfaces(_transitive_interfaces);
6361   ik->set_local_interfaces(_local_interfaces);
6362   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6363   _local_interfaces = NULL;
6364 
6365   // Initialize itable offset tables
6366   klassItable::setup_itable_offset_table(ik);
6367 
6368   // Compute transitive closure of interfaces this class implements
6369   // Do final class setup
6370   OopMapBlocksBuilder* oop_map_blocks = _field_info->oop_map_blocks;
6371   if (oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
6372     oop_map_blocks->copy(ik->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps());
6373   }
6374 
6375   if (_has_contended_fields || _parsed_annotations->is_contended() ||
6376       ( _super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_contended_annotations())) {
6377     ik->set_has_contended_annotations(true);
6378   }
6379 
6380   // Fill in has_finalizer, has_vanilla_constructor, and layout_helper
6381   set_precomputed_flags(ik);
6382 
6383   // check if this class can access its super class
6384   check_super_class_access(ik, CHECK);
6385 
6386   // check if this class can access its superinterfaces
6387   check_super_interface_access(ik, CHECK);
6388 
6389   // check if this class overrides any final method
6390   check_final_method_override(ik, CHECK);
6391 
6392   // reject static interface methods prior to Java 8
6393   if (ik->is_interface() && _major_version < JAVA_8_VERSION) {
6394     check_illegal_static_method(ik, CHECK);
6395   }
6396 
6397   // Obtain this_klass' module entry
6398   ModuleEntry* module_entry = ik->module();
6399   assert(module_entry != NULL, "module_entry should always be set");
6400 
6401   // Obtain java.lang.Module
6402   Handle module_handle(THREAD, module_entry->module());
6403 
6404   // Allocate mirror and initialize static fields
6405   // The create_mirror() call will also call compute_modifiers()
6406   java_lang_Class::create_mirror(ik,
6407                                  Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
6408                                  module_handle,
6409                                  _protection_domain,
6410                                  cl_inst_info.class_data(),
6411                                  CHECK);
6412 
6413   assert(_all_mirandas != NULL, "invariant");
6414 
6415   // Generate any default methods - default methods are public interface methods
6416   // that have a default implementation.  This is new with Java 8.
6417   if (_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
6418     DefaultMethods::generate_default_methods(ik,
6419                                              _all_mirandas,
6420                                              CHECK);
6421   }
6422 
6423   // Add read edges to the unnamed modules of the bootstrap and app class loaders.
6424   if (changed_by_loadhook && !module_handle.is_null() && module_entry->is_named() &&
6425       !module_entry->has_default_read_edges()) {
6426     if (!module_entry->set_has_default_read_edges()) {
6427       // We won a potential race
6428       JvmtiExport::add_default_read_edges(module_handle, THREAD);
6429     }
6430   }
6431 
6432   int nfields = ik->java_fields_count();
6433   if (ik->is_inline_klass()) nfields++;
6434   for (int i = 0; i < nfields; i++) {
6435     if (ik->field_is_inline_type(i)) {
6436       Symbol* klass_name = ik->field_signature(i)->fundamental_name(CHECK);
6437       // Inline classes for instance fields must have been pre-loaded
6438       // Inline classes for static fields might not have been loaded yet
6439       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::find(klass_name,
6440           Handle(THREAD, ik->class_loader()),
6441           Handle(THREAD, ik->protection_domain()), CHECK);
6442       if (klass != NULL) {
6443         assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(), "Inline type expected");
6444         ik->set_value_field_klass(i, klass);
6445       }
6446       klass_name->decrement_refcount();
6447     } else
6448       if (is_inline_type() && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_FIELD_INTERNAL) != 0)
6449         && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_STATIC) != 0)) {
6450       ValueKlass::cast(ik)->set_default_value_offset(ik->field_offset(i));
6451     }
6452   }
6453 
6454   if (is_inline_type()) {
6455     ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(ik);
6456     if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
6457       vk->set_alignment(_alignment);
6458       vk->set_first_field_offset(_first_field_offset);
6459       vk->set_exact_size_in_bytes(_exact_size_in_bytes);
6460     } else {
6461       vk->set_first_field_offset(vk->first_field_offset_old());
6462     }
6463     ValueKlass::cast(ik)->initialize_calling_convention(CHECK);
6464   }
6465 
6466   ClassLoadingService::notify_class_loaded(ik, false /* not shared class */);
6467 
6468   if (!is_internal()) {
6469     if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, load)) {
6470       ResourceMark rm;
6471       const char* module_name = (module_entry->name() == NULL) ? UNNAMED_MODULE : module_entry->name()->as_C_string();
6472       ik->print_class_load_logging(_loader_data, module_name, _stream);
6473     }
6474 
6475     if (ik->minor_version() == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
6476         ik->major_version() == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
6477         log_is_enabled(Info, class, preview)) {
6478       ResourceMark rm;
6479       log_info(class, preview)("Loading class %s that depends on preview features (class file version %d.65535)",
6480                                ik->external_name(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
6481     }
6482 
6483     if (log_is_enabled(Debug, class, resolve))  {
6484       ResourceMark rm;
6485       // print out the superclass.
6486       const char * from = ik->external_name();
6487       if (ik->java_super() != NULL) {
6488         log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (super)",
6489                    from,
6490                    ik->java_super()->external_name());
6491       }
6492       // print out each of the interface classes referred to by this class.
6493       const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = ik->local_interfaces();
6494       if (local_interfaces != NULL) {
6495         const int length = local_interfaces->length();
6496         for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
6497           const InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
6498           const char * to = k->external_name();
6499           log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (interface)", from, to);
6500         }
6501       }
6502     }
6503   }
6504 
6505   JFR_ONLY(INIT_ID(ik);)
6506 
6507   // If we reach here, all is well.
6508   // Now remove the InstanceKlass* from the _klass_to_deallocate field
6509   // in order for it to not be destroyed in the ClassFileParser destructor.
6510   set_klass_to_deallocate(NULL);
6511 
6512   // it's official
6513   set_klass(ik);
6514 
6515   if (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6516     Universe::initialize_the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array(ik, CHECK);
6517   }
6518 
6519   debug_only(ik->verify();)
6520 }
6521 
6522 void ClassFileParser::update_class_name(Symbol* new_class_name) {
6523   // Decrement the refcount in the old name, since we're clobbering it.
6524   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6525 
6526   _class_name = new_class_name;
6527   // Increment the refcount of the new name.
6528   // Now the ClassFileParser owns this name and will decrement in
6529   // the destructor.
6530   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6531 }
6532 
6533 // For an unsafe anonymous class that is in the unnamed package, move it to its host class's
6534 // package by prepending its host class's package name to its class name and setting
6535 // its _class_name field.
6536 void ClassFileParser::prepend_host_package_name(const InstanceKlass* unsafe_anonymous_host, TRAPS) {
6537   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6538   assert(strrchr(_class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) == NULL,
6539          "Unsafe anonymous class should not be in a package");
6540   TempNewSymbol host_pkg_name =
6541     ClassLoader::package_from_class_name(unsafe_anonymous_host->name());
6542 
6543   if (host_pkg_name != NULL) {
6544     int host_pkg_len = host_pkg_name->utf8_length();
6545     int class_name_len = _class_name->utf8_length();
6546     int symbol_len = host_pkg_len + 1 + class_name_len;
6547     char* new_anon_name = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(char, symbol_len + 1);
6548     int n = os::snprintf(new_anon_name, symbol_len + 1, "%.*s/%.*s",
6549                          host_pkg_len, host_pkg_name->base(), class_name_len, _class_name->base());
6550     assert(n == symbol_len, "Unexpected number of characters in string");
6551 
6552     // Decrement old _class_name to avoid leaking.
6553     _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6554 
6555     // Create a symbol and update the anonymous class name.
6556     // The new class name is created with a refcount of one. When installed into the InstanceKlass,
6557     // it'll be two and when the ClassFileParser destructor runs, it'll go back to one and get deleted
6558     // when the class is unloaded.
6559     _class_name = SymbolTable::new_symbol(new_anon_name, symbol_len);
6560   }
6561 }
6562 
6563 // If the host class and the anonymous class are in the same package then do
6564 // nothing.  If the anonymous class is in the unnamed package then move it to its
6565 // host's package.  If the classes are in different packages then throw an IAE
6566 // exception.
6567 void ClassFileParser::fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(TRAPS) {
6568   assert(_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL, "Expected an unsafe anonymous class");
6569 
6570   const jbyte* anon_last_slash = UTF8::strrchr((const jbyte*)_class_name->base(),
6571                                                _class_name->utf8_length(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH);
6572   if (anon_last_slash == NULL) {  // Unnamed package
6573     prepend_host_package_name(_unsafe_anonymous_host, CHECK);
6574   } else {
6575     if (!_unsafe_anonymous_host->is_same_class_package(_unsafe_anonymous_host->class_loader(), _class_name)) {
6576       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6577       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalArgumentException(),
6578         err_msg("Host class %s and anonymous class %s are in different packages",
6579         _unsafe_anonymous_host->name()->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string()));
6580     }
6581   }
6582 }
6583 
6584 static bool relax_format_check_for(ClassLoaderData* loader_data) {
6585   bool trusted = loader_data->is_boot_class_loader_data() ||
6586                  loader_data->is_platform_class_loader_data();
6587   bool need_verify =
6588     // verifyAll
6589     (BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote) ||
6590     // verifyRemote
6591     (!BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote && !trusted);
6592   return !need_verify;
6593 }
6594 
6595 ClassFileParser::ClassFileParser(ClassFileStream* stream,
6596                                  Symbol* name,
6597                                  ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
6598                                  const ClassLoadInfo* cl_info,
6599                                  Publicity pub_level,
6600                                  TRAPS) :
6601   _stream(stream),
6602   _class_name(NULL),
6603   _loader_data(loader_data),
6604   _unsafe_anonymous_host(cl_info->unsafe_anonymous_host()),
6605   _cp_patches(cl_info->cp_patches()),
6606   _is_hidden(cl_info->is_hidden()),
6607   _can_access_vm_annotations(cl_info->can_access_vm_annotations()),
6608   _num_patched_klasses(0),
6609   _max_num_patched_klasses(0),
6610   _orig_cp_size(0),
6611   _first_patched_klass_resolved_index(0),
6612   _super_klass(),
6613   _cp(NULL),
6614   _fields(NULL),
6615   _methods(NULL),
6616   _inner_classes(NULL),
6617   _nest_members(NULL),
6618   _nest_host(0),
6619   _permitted_subclasses(NULL),
6620   _record_components(NULL),
6621   _temp_local_interfaces(NULL),
6622   _local_interfaces(NULL),
6623   _transitive_interfaces(NULL),
6624   _combined_annotations(NULL),
6625   _class_annotations(NULL),
6626   _class_type_annotations(NULL),
6627   _fields_annotations(NULL),
6628   _fields_type_annotations(NULL),
6629   _klass(NULL),
6630   _klass_to_deallocate(NULL),
6631   _parsed_annotations(NULL),
6632   _fac(NULL),
6633   _field_info(NULL),
6634   _method_ordering(NULL),
6635   _all_mirandas(NULL),
6636   _vtable_size(0),
6637   _itable_size(0),
6638   _num_miranda_methods(0),
6639   _rt(REF_NONE),
6640   _protection_domain(cl_info->protection_domain()),
6641   _access_flags(),
6642   _pub_level(pub_level),
6643   _bad_constant_seen(0),
6644   _synthetic_flag(false),
6645   _sde_length(false),
6646   _sde_buffer(NULL),
6647   _sourcefile_index(0),
6648   _generic_signature_index(0),
6649   _major_version(0),
6650   _minor_version(0),
6651   _this_class_index(0),
6652   _super_class_index(0),
6653   _itfs_len(0),
6654   _java_fields_count(0),
6655   _need_verify(false),
6656   _relax_verify(false),
6657   _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6658   _declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6659   _has_final_method(false),
6660   _has_contended_fields(false),
6661   _has_inline_type_fields(false),
6662   _has_nonstatic_fields(false),
6663   _is_empty_inline_type(false),
6664   _is_naturally_atomic(false),
6665   _is_declared_atomic(false),
6666   _invalid_inline_super(false),
6667   _invalid_identity_super(false),
6668   _implements_identityObject(false),
6669   _has_injected_identityObject(false),
6670   _has_finalizer(false),
6671   _has_empty_finalizer(false),
6672   _has_vanilla_constructor(false),
6673   _max_bootstrap_specifier_index(-1) {
6674 
6675   _class_name = name != NULL ? name : vmSymbols::unknown_class_name();
6676   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6677 
6678   assert(THREAD->is_Java_thread(), "invariant");
6679   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
6680   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6681   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
6682   assert(_stream->buffer() == _stream->current(), "invariant");
6683   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6684   assert(0 == _access_flags.as_int(), "invariant");
6685 
6686   // Figure out whether we can skip format checking (matching classic VM behavior)
6687   if (DumpSharedSpaces) {
6688     // verify == true means it's a 'remote' class (i.e., non-boot class)
6689     // Verification decision is based on BytecodeVerificationRemote flag
6690     // for those classes.
6691     _need_verify = (stream->need_verify()) ? BytecodeVerificationRemote :
6692                                               BytecodeVerificationLocal;
6693   }
6694   else {
6695     _need_verify = Verifier::should_verify_for(_loader_data->class_loader(),
6696                                                stream->need_verify());
6697   }
6698   if (_cp_patches != NULL) {
6699     int len = _cp_patches->length();
6700     for (int i=0; i<len; i++) {
6701       if (has_cp_patch_at(i)) {
6702         Handle patch = cp_patch_at(i);
6703         if (java_lang_String::is_instance(patch()) || java_lang_Class::is_instance(patch())) {
6704           // We need to append the names of the patched classes to the end of the constant pool,
6705           // because a patched class may have a Utf8 name that's not already included in the
6706           // original constant pool. These class names are used when patch_constant_pool()
6707           // calls patch_class().
6708           //
6709           // Note that a String in cp_patch_at(i) may be used to patch a Utf8, a String, or a Class.
6710           // At this point, we don't know the tag for index i yet, because we haven't parsed the
6711           // constant pool. So we can only assume the worst -- every String is used to patch a Class.
6712           _max_num_patched_klasses++;
6713         }
6714       }
6715     }
6716   }
6717 
6718   // synch back verification state to stream
6719   stream->set_verify(_need_verify);
6720 
6721   // Check if verification needs to be relaxed for this class file
6722   // Do not restrict it to jdk1.0 or jdk1.1 to maintain backward compatibility (4982376)
6723   _relax_verify = relax_format_check_for(_loader_data);
6724 
6725   parse_stream(stream, CHECK);
6726 
6727   post_process_parsed_stream(stream, _cp, CHECK);
6728 }
6729 
6730 void ClassFileParser::clear_class_metadata() {
6731   // metadata created before the instance klass is created.  Must be
6732   // deallocated if classfile parsing returns an error.
6733   _cp = NULL;
6734   _fields = NULL;
6735   _methods = NULL;
6736   _inner_classes = NULL;
6737   _nest_members = NULL;
6738   _permitted_subclasses = NULL;
6739   _combined_annotations = NULL;
6740   _class_annotations = _class_type_annotations = NULL;
6741   _fields_annotations = _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
6742   _record_components = NULL;
6743 }
6744 
6745 // Destructor to clean up
6746 ClassFileParser::~ClassFileParser() {
6747   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6748 
6749   if (_cp != NULL) {
6750     MetadataFactory::free_metadata(_loader_data, _cp);
6751   }
6752   if (_fields != NULL) {
6753     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _fields);
6754   }
6755 
6756   if (_methods != NULL) {
6757     // Free methods
6758     InstanceKlass::deallocate_methods(_loader_data, _methods);
6759   }
6760 
6761   // beware of the Universe::empty_blah_array!!
6762   if (_inner_classes != NULL && _inner_classes != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6763     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _inner_classes);
6764   }
6765 
6766   if (_nest_members != NULL && _nest_members != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6767     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _nest_members);
6768   }
6769 
6770   if (_record_components != NULL) {
6771     InstanceKlass::deallocate_record_components(_loader_data, _record_components);
6772   }
6773 
6774   if (_permitted_subclasses != NULL && _permitted_subclasses != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6775     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _permitted_subclasses);
6776   }
6777 
6778   // Free interfaces
6779   InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(_loader_data, _super_klass,
6780                                        _local_interfaces, _transitive_interfaces);
6781 
6782   if (_combined_annotations != NULL) {
6783     // After all annotations arrays have been created, they are installed into the
6784     // Annotations object that will be assigned to the InstanceKlass being created.
6785 
6786     // Deallocate the Annotations object and the installed annotations arrays.
6787     _combined_annotations->deallocate_contents(_loader_data);
6788 
6789     // If the _combined_annotations pointer is non-NULL,
6790     // then the other annotations fields should have been cleared.
6791     assert(_class_annotations       == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6792     assert(_class_type_annotations  == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6793     assert(_fields_annotations      == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6794     assert(_fields_type_annotations == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6795   } else {
6796     // If the annotations arrays were not installed into the Annotations object,
6797     // then they have to be deallocated explicitly.
6798     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_annotations);
6799     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_type_annotations);
6800     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_annotations);
6801     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_type_annotations);
6802   }
6803 
6804   clear_class_metadata();
6805   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6806   _local_interfaces = NULL;
6807 
6808   // deallocate the klass if already created.  Don't directly deallocate, but add
6809   // to the deallocate list so that the klass is removed from the CLD::_klasses list
6810   // at a safepoint.
6811   if (_klass_to_deallocate != NULL) {
6812     _loader_data->add_to_deallocate_list(_klass_to_deallocate);
6813   }
6814 }
6815 
6816 void ClassFileParser::parse_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
6817                                    TRAPS) {
6818 
6819   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6820   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6821 
6822   // BEGIN STREAM PARSING
6823   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // magic, major, minor
6824   // Magic value
6825   const u4 magic = stream->get_u4_fast();
6826   guarantee_property(magic == JAVA_CLASSFILE_MAGIC,
6827                      "Incompatible magic value %u in class file %s",
6828                      magic, CHECK);
6829 
6830   // Version numbers
6831   _minor_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6832   _major_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6833 
6834   if (DumpSharedSpaces && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6835     ResourceMark rm;
6836     warning("Pre JDK 6 class not supported by CDS: %u.%u %s",
6837             _major_version,  _minor_version, _class_name->as_C_string());
6838     Exceptions::fthrow(
6839       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6840       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
6841       "Unsupported major.minor version for dump time %u.%u",
6842       _major_version,
6843       _minor_version);
6844   }
6845 
6846   // Check version numbers - we check this even with verifier off
6847   verify_class_version(_major_version, _minor_version, _class_name, CHECK);
6848 
6849   stream->guarantee_more(3, CHECK); // length, first cp tag
6850   u2 cp_size = stream->get_u2_fast();
6851 
6852   guarantee_property(
6853     cp_size >= 1, "Illegal constant pool size %u in class file %s",
6854     cp_size, CHECK);
6855 
6856   _orig_cp_size = cp_size;
6857   if (is_hidden()) { // Add a slot for hidden class name.
6858     assert(_max_num_patched_klasses == 0, "Sanity check");
6859     cp_size++;
6860   } else {
6861     if (int(cp_size) + _max_num_patched_klasses > 0xffff) {
6862       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_InternalError(), "not enough space for patched classes");
6863     }
6864     cp_size += _max_num_patched_klasses;
6865   }
6866 
6867   _cp = ConstantPool::allocate(_loader_data,
6868                                cp_size,
6869                                CHECK);
6870 
6871   ConstantPool* const cp = _cp;
6872 
6873   parse_constant_pool(stream, cp, _orig_cp_size, CHECK);
6874 
6875   assert(cp_size == (const u2)cp->length(), "invariant");
6876 
6877   // ACCESS FLAGS
6878   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // flags, this_class, super_class, infs_len
6879 
6880   jint recognized_modifiers = JVM_RECOGNIZED_CLASS_MODIFIERS;
6881   // JVM_ACC_MODULE is defined in JDK-9 and later.
6882   if (_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION) {
6883     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_MODULE;
6884   }
6885   // JVM_ACC_VALUE is defined for class file version 55 and later
6886   if (supports_inline_types()) {
6887     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_VALUE;
6888   }
6889 
6890   // Access flags
6891   jint flags = stream->get_u2_fast() & recognized_modifiers;
6892 
6893   if ((flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE) && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6894     // Set abstract bit for old class files for backward compatibility
6895     flags |= JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT;
6896   }
6897 
6898   verify_legal_class_modifiers(flags, CHECK);
6899 
6900   short bad_constant = class_bad_constant_seen();
6901   if (bad_constant != 0) {
6902     // Do not throw CFE until after the access_flags are checked because if
6903     // ACC_MODULE is set in the access flags, then NCDFE must be thrown, not CFE.
6904     classfile_parse_error("Unknown constant tag %u in class file %s", bad_constant, CHECK);
6905   }
6906 
6907   _access_flags.set_flags(flags);
6908 
6909   // This class and superclass
6910   _this_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6911   check_property(
6912     valid_cp_range(_this_class_index, cp_size) &&
6913       cp->tag_at(_this_class_index).is_unresolved_klass(),
6914     "Invalid this class index %u in constant pool in class file %s",
6915     _this_class_index, CHECK);
6916 
6917   Symbol* const class_name_in_cp = cp->klass_name_at(_this_class_index);
6918   assert(class_name_in_cp != NULL, "class_name can't be null");
6919 
6920   // Don't need to check whether this class name is legal or not.
6921   // It has been checked when constant pool is parsed.
6922   // However, make sure it is not an array type.
6923   if (_need_verify) {
6924     guarantee_property(class_name_in_cp->char_at(0) != JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY,
6925                        "Bad class name in class file %s",
6926                        CHECK);
6927   }
6928 
6929 #ifdef ASSERT
6930   // Basic sanity checks
6931   assert(!(_is_hidden && (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL)), "mutually exclusive variants");
6932 
6933   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6934     assert(_class_name == vmSymbols::unknown_class_name(), "A named anonymous class???");
6935   }
6936   if (_is_hidden) {
6937     assert(_class_name != vmSymbols::unknown_class_name(), "hidden classes should have a special name");
6938   }
6939 #endif
6940 
6941   // Update the _class_name as needed depending on whether this is a named,
6942   // un-named, hidden or unsafe-anonymous class.
6943 
6944   if (_is_hidden) {
6945     assert(_class_name != NULL, "Unexpected null _class_name");
6946 #ifdef ASSERT
6947     if (_need_verify) {
6948       verify_legal_class_name(_class_name, CHECK);
6949     }
6950 #endif
6951 
6952   // NOTE: !_is_hidden does not imply "findable" as it could be an old-style
6953   //       "hidden" unsafe-anonymous class
6954 
6955   // If this is an anonymous class fix up its name if it is in the unnamed
6956   // package.  Otherwise, throw IAE if it is in a different package than
6957   // its host class.
6958   } else if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6959     update_class_name(class_name_in_cp);
6960     fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(CHECK);
6961 
6962   } else {
6963     // Check if name in class file matches given name
6964     if (_class_name != class_name_in_cp) {
6965       if (_class_name != vmSymbols::unknown_class_name()) {
6966         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6967         Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6968                            vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
